Chen and Liu's Mission to Japan

(Nanjing) Various Chinese and foreign newspapers have recorded many different versions of Chen Youren and Liu Jiwen's trip to Japan. Yesterday, I met a certain foreigner who said that the rumors that Chen and others were carrying certain conditions to Japan were not so simple in fact. However, it would not be believable to say that Chen and others' trip to Japan had no political relationship. It is said that the motive for this matter was at the end of June. At that time, the old and new factions in Guangzhou were not very united, and they were also worried about the lack of diplomatic support, making it difficult to achieve anything. Therefore, it was decided to temporarily use any means to first take advantage of a certain country in order to obtain diplomatic and military convenience. After the position was consolidated, the policy would be changed. On the other hand, a certain country, based on its traditional policy of not wanting China to be united, was happy to accept this. At that time, the Korean Incident had not yet occurred, and signals had already been sent to important figures of a certain country stationed in Guangdong. That country gladly agreed and promised to provide informal hospitality. After the Korean Incident occurred, this previously agreed plan could not be withdrawn. Therefore, Chen and Liu visited Japan as originally planned, but at this time, it was just an exchange of opinions. The truth is like this. (27th Special Dispatch)

Ministry of Railways Convenes Two-Line Defense Conference

Pay Attention to the Safety of Important People Traveling by Train

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Railways convened a two-line defense conference on the 27th. Representatives from the Capital Garrison Headquarters and the Police Department attended. It was decided to implement the following measures in Nanjing: (1) Inspections will continue as before. (2) Railway police will be responsible for maintaining traffic order and the joint military police will be responsible for security inside and outside the station. (3) Inspections by other agencies will still take place outside the station. (4) A separate route will be designated at Nanjing Station specifically for the use of important figures. Additional train police will be stationed for protection. A special waiting room will be set up upstairs in the station for important figures to rest. (27th Special Dispatch)

Liu Dajun Discusses Silver Prices

(Nanjing) Recent foreign news reported that the Mexican government had decided to adopt a silver standard, and that Germany was also preparing to mint a large quantity of silver auxiliary coins. According to the opinion of statistics expert Liu Dajun, Mexico is a silver-producing country and also a colony of the United States. If it adopts a silver standard, it will be very unfavorable to the United States. Whether the United States will recognize it is a question. Even if it is possible, it will only increase the use of silver to some extent. Its impact on China's economy will only be to slightly stabilize the silver market. The reason for the cheapness of silver in the world is actually due to the rise in prices and the lack of gold production. The main gold-producing area in the world is South Africa. According to experts, South African gold mines are nearing exhaustion. The issue of gold use in the future is a very big problem. As for China, it is currently necessary to first seek the stability of silver prices and prevent gold prices from continuing to rise. In order to conform to the world trend, it is necessary to adopt the gold standard. (27th Special Dispatch)

Important Foreign Telegrams

Diplomatic Negotiations Between Britain, the United States, and Germany

Related to Financial Issues

MacDonald Changes to Train to Go to Berlin

Stimson Leaves Germany for Britain

Increasing Trust in the Germans

▲Reuters, London, 26th—British Prime Minister MacDonald departs for Berlin by train tonight because the weather is not favorable for aviation. Foreign Secretary Henderson and officials from the ministry departed this morning. The German Prime Minister and Foreign Minister previously visited London and stayed briefly at the British Prime Minister's villa. The British Prime Minister and others are now visiting the German capital in return.

▲National, Berlin, 27th—British Foreign Secretary Henderson arrived here at 8:30 this morning. After getting off the train, he told reporters of his joy in visiting, saying that visiting Germany at this difficult time for Germany is deeply symbolic of the friendship between the two countries. He then drove to the specially prepared Grand Emperor Hotel. British Prime Minister MacDonald will also stay there after arriving in Berlin tonight. Afterward, US Secretary of State Stimson, after meeting with the German President, immediately drove to visit Henderson. Afterward, he boarded a train for London at 1:00 PM. Before leaving, Stimson spoke to reporters, praising the German Prime Minister Brüning and his cabinet members for their courage and determination, and expressing great admiration. He also said that before coming to Berlin, he had great trust in the ability of the German people to extricate themselves from their financial difficulties. The US government and people also share this trust. What he has seen and heard since coming to Berlin is sufficient to prove this trust.

▲Reuters, Berlin, 26th—After consulting with representatives from the German government and national banks, major German banks decided to establish an "Acceptance and Guarantee Bank" with a capital of 200,000,000 marks. The main purpose is to restore the unobstructed flow of national currency and to support the resumption of business of the closed National Bank. Everyone expressed satisfaction, as this proposal proves Germany's sincerity in striving to restore world credit. Therefore, the National Bank can relax its current restrictive methods that prevent industry and commerce from operating. German Prime Minister Brüning and US Secretary of State Stimson had an informal and confidential discussion over lunch in Potsdam, discussing this and other matters. The diplomatic community attaches great importance to this discussion.

▲National, Berlin, 26th—Swedish banker Wallenberg and American advisor Spag to the Bank of England arrived in Berlin today to discuss with the German government how to implement the resolutions of the seven-nation conference in London. It is expected that bankers from various countries will arrive in Germany one after another, and the discussion period may take a month. According to reports, Wallenberg and Spag expressed admiration for the German bankers' joint creation of an acceptance and mortgage guarantee bank. The establishment of this type of bank has also won praise in domestic public opinion.

Strange Flyers Spread in Germany's Northern Industrial Area

Predicting a Great Revolution in Germany

The World Will Be Reddened

The Fall of Capitalism

Presumed to Be the Work of Radicals

▲National, Berlin, 26th—A peculiar flyer was found in Germany's northern industrial area today, predicting that a great revolution would occur in Germany on August 1st, the day the European war began. This flyer was mimeographed, and it is unknown where it came from. After the police discovered it, it was impossible to track down the mastermind. Although it is regarded by the political circles as a kind of nonsense used to incite the people, the newspapers say that this matter cannot be taken as merely accidental. Because Novotny, the signer of the flyer, described the events after the revolution in great detail and in accordance with Marxism, it is probably the instigation of radicals to disturb the people, so it cannot be taken lightly. According to the flyer's predictions, the vanguard of national socialism will occupy Wilhelm Street on August 1st. At the same time, members of parliament will gather in the Reichstag to declare the establishment of the Third Reich. But this dictatorial government will only last for three days. On August 5th, the Red Army from the Ruhr area will attack the capital, defeat Hitler's army, and Russian cavalry will invade Poland at the same time. The Polish army will inevitably disintegrate. Then the Soviet governments of Russia, Poland, and Germany will form an alliance, gathering the natural resources of the three countries to resist capitalist countries. It is expected that within 48 hours, Norway, Sweden, Denmark, and the Balkan countries will join this alliance, and dictatorship in Italy will be overthrown within a day or two. Communism will soon invade France, then England from France, and capitalist governments will be overthrown one by one. Even Fiji will be governed by the Zulu and Arab people. After the Soviet government of England abandons its suzerainty over India, India will eliminate princes and become independent. Novotny's predictions for China say that Siam and Vietnam will inevitably return to China in the future, and the abolition of China's existing consular jurisdiction and concessions will not require any effort.

Chilean President Resigns

Four Years of Autocracy, Public Resentment Boils Over

▲Reuters, Chilean Capital, 26th—Chilean President Ibáñez resigned today to avoid bloodshed, ending four years of autocracy. Three cabinet members have resigned this month due to popular discontent. Indian Authorities Coerce the Collection of Land Taxes

Court Magistrate Assassinated

▲Reuters, Calcutta, 27th—Garlick, the upper-level magistrate of Alipore District in Calcutta, was shot and killed in court today. The assassin was also shot and killed by the police.

Royal Austro-Hungarian Marriage

Contains Political Motives

▲ Nanjing Dispatch, 26th: Princess Ileana of Romania, the youngest sister of the King of Romania, was married here today to Archduke Anton of the House of Habsburg. They plan to reside in Vienna after the marriage. According to official reports, the marriage is purely out of love, but observers of the political situation mostly believe it contains political motives. The current King of Romania often expresses sympathy for Hungary. If the Habsburg monarchy in Hungary is restored in the future after this marriage, the two countries will become closely linked. Therefore, it is believed that the King of Romania may intend to break away from the Little Entente and form a political and commercial alliance with Hungary. Now that Germany and Austria have a customs union plan, if Romania and Hungary combine and become close to Germany, the remaining two countries of the Little Entente (Czechoslovakia and Yugoslavia) will also be forced to take the same path. If such a situation of Central European consolidation is achieved, France will be isolated. Looking around Europe, only Poland can be considered a strong ally. This is related to the rise and fall of German and French power, and today's marriage of the Romanian princess may be the first cornerstone in building this edifice. It is also possible. (Translator's note: Romania and Hungary are agricultural countries, suffering from a lack of sales channels for agricultural products. Germany is an industrial country, while France is a semi-agricultural and semi-industrial country. Therefore, after the implementation of the German-Austrian customs union, it is likely to extend to Hungary and Romania.)

Chen Youren's Mission to Japan

Received with Gentlemanly Courtesy

Foreign Ministry Issues Statement

▲ Tokyo Dispatch from the Dentsu News Agency, 27th: It is rumored that Chen Youren's purpose in going to Japan is to hire six Japanese officers below the rank of colonel as military advisors.

▲ Tokyo Dispatch from the Dentsu News Agency, 27th: Chen Youren entered Tokyo on the 26th. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs issued a statement on the 26th, stating that "Signs of political turmoil in China are emerging again. Therefore, it is not surprising that many famous Chinese come to Japan. If these Chinese who come to Japan do not engage in political activities in their own country, it is only natural that Japan treats them with due respect. Even if Mr. Chen Youren's arrival in Tokyo is a fact, although it is not at the instigation of the Japanese government and is not based on the intentions of the Japanese government, it is still natural to treat him as a foreign gentleman with due courtesy. The Japanese government's attitude towards the internal chaos in China has been repeatedly stated and remains unchanged."

▲ Tokyo Dispatch from Reuters, 27th: It is heard that the military authorities have received a telegram from Guangzhou, intending to hire seven junior officers as military advisors and several senior craftsmen from arsenals. They have also requested the supply of military equipment and ammunition. It is heard that the military authorities seem likely to reject this request, fearing it will cause disputes with the Nanjing government, as the Nanjing government has already been officially recognized as the sole government of China. Chen Youren will return here tonight. It is heard that he will visit Foreign Minister Baron Kijūrō Shidehara and other officials. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs intends to treat him as an ordinary foreign traveler.

Dark Photographs of American Prisons

▲ Washington Dispatch from Reuters, 27th: The report of the U.S. Prison Investigation Committee states that most prisons, despite implementing unbelievably harsh punishments, ultimately fail to achieve rehabilitation. In the future, a new organizational law should be used, education should be vigorously implemented, and prison officials should be people capable of managing schools. The report mentions the tragic conditions in prisons, stating that juvenile offenders are often subjected to severe beatings, almost to the point of death, and are not only shackled but also immersed in cold water, sometimes deprived of food and drink. The prison hospitals are often full of patients, and the only one that is managed reasonably well is the Idaho Industrial Training School. It also states that juvenile offenders should not be treated the same as adult felons.

Nagata Comet Approaching Earth

Visible in a Few Months

▲ California Dispatch from Dentsu News Agency, 26th: The Wilson Observatory announced today that the comet discovered by Nagata, a Japanese American, will gradually approach Earth in a few months and will be visible to the naked eye. However, the exact date has not yet been calculated. Nagata, who discovered the comet, is a poor artist residing in Bulura, California. He observed the sky several weeks ago and unexpectedly discovered a new comet in the Leo constellation. He reported it to the Wilson Observatory, which confirmed it and named it the Nagata Comet.

Dutch Doctor Discovers New Cancer Diagnosis

Good News for the Medical Community

▲ London Dispatch from Reuters, 26th: Bensegn, a previously little-known Dutch doctor, has been engaged in research work for many years and is now a world-class cancer expert. Dr. Bensegn claims that he can diagnose cancer using blood tests. A representative of the British Empire Cancer Research Association, Kenginenai, personally went to Zist to investigate his experiments and has just returned to London. According to him,

This is the greatest advancement in understanding cancer in fifty years. Dr. Bensegn's diagnostic method is now immediately being used in the London Cancer Hospital. According to opinions in the British medical community, Dr. Bensegn's new invention, although not a new treatment method, is extremely valuable.

Telegram from Zhangjiakou

Respectfully to all newspaper offices: Recently, a telegram was sent to the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, forwarded to the generals and soldiers at the front lines fighting against the Communists. The telegram reads: "Heaven has brought disaster to the Yellow race, and the poison of the Red flames flows. Across the territories of the four remaining provinces of Hunan, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Guangdong, the Communists are digging their graves and burying everything. Millions of compatriots are drowning together. Communist forces are everywhere, and houses are in ruins. The red flag flies, and the people suffer. Compared to Li Zicheng and Zhang Xianzhong, the killings are even more numerous. Compared to Zhu Ci and Huang Chao, the brutality is even worse. If they are not eradicated in time, our sacred Chinese nation of five thousand years will be completely plunged into a place of fire and water, and ten thousand eons of no recovery. The central government embraces the wish of compassion for all and is deeply concerned about the dangers of weapons and death. Therefore, we raise a righteous army and launch a large-scale campaign of suppression. Our commander-in-chief braves the summer heat and marches quickly, concerned for the country. Our generals and soldiers are generous and determined to fulfill their missions and vow to establish merit. Wherever we go, we should be invincible, like pulling down dry leaves. Our prestige should spread far and wide, and the people should be freed from their suffering. Victory reports should be frequent, and both heaven and man should admire us. We humbly request that you carry forward the spirit of great fearlessness, continue your efforts, establish a unified foundation as solid as a rock, thoroughly implement our policies, eliminate all traces of the bandits, alleviate the suffering of our people, and not only comfort the spirit of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen in heaven but also comfort the hopes of people all over the world. The South is looking up, and the North is leaning in. We respectfully present our humble regards and eagerly anticipate your response, hoping that you will send a telegram of encouragement to inspire us. We are filled with anticipation. Sincerely, Liu Yifei, Chairman of the Chahar Provincial Government; Committee Members Jian Yong, Wen Guang, Gao Xibing, Zhao Xingde, Hang Jinshou, and Demuchukezhenglupu, together kowtowing in Qinyuan."

What is most noteworthy in the above table is that among the 560,091 Koreans residing in the three northeastern provinces in 1930, only 38,163 resided in areas under Japanese jurisdiction, such as the affiliated territories or treaty ports, and within the land used by the Chinese Eastern Railway. A staggering 521,929 Koreans had penetrated deep into the northeastern hinterland, coexisting with our people. These Koreans who had penetrated deep into our country's hinterland almost exclusively engaged in the cultivation of paddy and dryland rice fields. Moreover, their distribution areas were all fertile land with convenient water sources and good soil. These uninvited guests who came in groups were no less than formidable enemies who were seizing the means of survival of the people of our Northeast. Such a serious problem, if not noticed and resolved early, is either a sign of blindness or foolishness.

Important News

Central and National Government Memorial Week

▲ Wang Boling speaks about pacifying internal affairs to resist foreign aggression and the situation in Yunnan

▲ Cai Yuanpei reports on three matters: suppression of the Communists, Shi You-san's rebellion, and the flood disaster

▲ Central Party Headquarters: The Central Party Headquarters held its 122nd Memorial Week at 9:00 AM on the 27th. Central Committee members Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Ding Weifen, Yu Jingtang, Wang Boling, Miao Peicheng, Fang Juehui, and over 600 staff and guests attended. Ding Weifen presided over the meeting. After the rituals, Wang Boling reported, stating that the current internal rebellion, foreign aggression, and Communist disaster are all resonating. Although the surface appears serious, pacifying internal affairs can resist foreign aggression. If internal rebellions do not occur, foreign aggression will not come. Shi You-san's rebellion was definitely colluding with Japanese imperialists behind the scenes, who were assisting with money. Moreover, if he managed to reach Pingjin, they even planned to assist with weapons and ammunition. The Guangdong faction also sent Chen Youren and Liu Jiwen to Japan to negotiate treasonous treaties and offer various benefits to the Japanese in order to plot rebellion. At this time, the Wanpaoshan Incident occurred, so foreign aggression was entirely caused by internal rebellion. Now, we should first eliminate the Communist disaster and punish the rebels. The central government and the Northeast have dispatched large armies to encircle Shi's rebellion. It can be resolved within ten days. The Guangdong faction is entangled with party issues. The party's righteousness must be displayed. If there is righteousness, then no one will dare to rebel again. This time's Guangdong coup was first corrected by Yunnan's telegram, which is very important. I have been to Yunnan twice and would like to briefly report on the situation in Yunnan. To understand the situation of party affairs in Yunnan and the needs for future construction, it is necessary to be familiar with Yunnan's environment, as well as the political, economic, transportation, and various recent conditions. Yunnan belonged to Chinese territory as early as 3,000 years ago, but it has always been laissez-faire. It was not until Zhu Yuanzhang's brother, Duke Mu of the Ming Dynasty, arrived in Yunnan and felt that the population was too small that he decided to immigrate and populate the border. He moved three million people from Jiangnan to Yunnan, distributed throughout the province, to recuperate and multiply. Over the years, many indigenous people have also assimilated. Unfortunately, immigration is still too small, so there are still quite a few semi-civilized indigenous people. Geographically speaking, no one can know the exact area of Yunnan. The ground is mostly mountainous. Some journeys of thirty days still do not leave the county. The size of the area can be imagined. It borders Myanmar to the west. The demarcation of the border between Myanmar and Yunnan is still pending. Since the British built a railway to Jiangxinpo and Pianma, the area west of Gaoligong Mountain is no longer ours. The British have also built a highway thousands of miles long, directly reaching Tibet. The future of Tibet is also very dangerous. It borders Annam to the south. When the border was demarcated, due to the昏庸 [lit. muddle-headed] of the Manchu court, more than three thousand miles of land were abandoned. In the early Republic of China, the strict prohibition of opium led people to move the border at night, and a lot was lost again. In addition, it is bordered by Guangxi and Guizhou to the east and Sichuan to the north. There is a lot of miasma. Since the Xinhai Revolution, the people of Yunnan have been able to manage the affairs of Yunnan. Cai Songpo (Cai E) made many achievements in Yunnan. There has been no major progress since then. Initially, transportation from Hunan and Sichuan to Yunnan took two months. After the sea ban was lifted, it was possible to travel from Hong Kong to Haiphong by train in one and a half days, then to the border, and then by Yunnan train to Kunming. This is the throat of Yunnan's access to the outside world, entirely controlled by the French, who levy heavy taxes on all goods that pass through, viewing us with the eyes of colonizers, thus further reducing the production in the interior of Yunnan. Therefore, road construction is very necessary. Currently, Yunnan can build over a thousand miles of highway a year, but due to limited manpower and financial resources, it has not been able to actively proceed. When it comes to finance, there is the Fuye Bank, which specializes in domestic and foreign exchange. In addition, there is the French Banque de l'Indochine, which issues banknotes and absorbs cash, resulting in higher exchange rates. Regarding the climate, the provincial capital is neither cold nor hot, but there are extremely hot places on the border, and the northwest is extremely cold, with snow for half the year. The province's products include items from cold, hot, and temperate zones. Mineral resources are particularly rich. The people are simple, hardworking, and hard-working. In Yunnan's party affairs, there were many comrades in the Tongmenghui (Revolutionary Alliance). Since Tang Jiyao sang the heresy of provincial autonomy, he broke away from our party. This was the situation from 1923 to 1925. After the Northern Expedition, there was the political change in 1927, and Tang Jiyao stepped down. At that time, the Guangdong Political Branch sent people to form the party, but unfortunately, they mistakenly sent communists. Suspicion and disputes arose, and Hu Ruoyu took the opportunity to instigate political turmoil. After the efforts of Comrade Long Yun to suppress the rebellion, it was finally pacified. As for today, party disputes have arisen again. Old comrades, CCP members, and those sent by the central government have each formed a provincial party headquarters, and there were three provincial party headquarters for a time. Later, the people from the central government and the old comrades combined to overthrow the communists, but then they split again. The central government decided to withdraw everyone and re-register. After my first inspection, I re-appointed guiding committee members and established the current provincial party headquarters. After a year of work, significant achievements have been made. Several communist organizations have been cracked down, so there is no possibility of the communists reviving in Yunnan. By the time of my second inspection of Yunnan, 14 lower-level party headquarters had been established. Over 200 mass organizations were also formed, and the atmosphere of opposing French imperialism was also quite激昂 [lit. impassioned]. Government officials have developed a great faith in the party, and the people's thoughts are leaning towards the Three Principles of the People. When the Guangdong coup occurred this time, Yunnan took the lead in advocating justice and refuted it. This is an important manifestation. If the whole country can be like this, then the country will be stable, and foreign aggressors will not be able to take advantage of the opportunity. Therefore, it is a profound truth to say that pacifying internal affairs can resist foreign aggression." The meeting adjourned after the report.

▲ National Government: The National Government held Memorial Week at 10:00 AM on the same morning. Yu Youren, Cai Yuanpei, Zhu Peide, Wang Boqun, Li Shuhua, Gao Weiyue, Ma Fuxiang, Ru Yuli, and over 200 other people attended. Yu Youren presided over the meeting. Cai

The most notable event for the people is naturally the Korean tragedy. I have already discussed my observations on this tragedy in the previous memorial week meeting held at the Central Party Headquarters, and all the newspapers have already published it, so everyone knows it, and I won't repeat it. Domestically, the most important thing is still the suppression of bandits in Jiangxi. The Red bandits are different from ordinary bandits; they have a well-defined and justified ideology, and they both threaten and entice the masses, seemingly possessing a kind of religious magic. Therefore, they should not be underestimated. They have secret organizations in various provinces, which are being cracked down on under the supervision of our party. In Jiangxi, they have already occupied territory and formed a Red Army, which is like adding wings to a tiger, creating endless troubles. According to the reports we have received, the Commander-in-Chief's prestige, the soldiers' bravery, and the rapid advance despite the summer heat have led to the recovery of all the important cities occupied by the Red bandits. Only their old nest of Donggu remains, and it will be captured soon. It will not be difficult to clip the tiger's wings. However, the Red bandits are like a plague wherever they go. Even if the plague is eliminated, its toxins remain, and a period of disinfection is necessary. This is the work of propaganda, which should thoroughly expose the bandits' fallacies so that the masses will not be fooled again. To truly awaken the masses, we must not only rely on theory but also give them practical strength. After eliminating the Red bandits from a certain place, if we do not make positive arrangements and simply return to the former state of corrupt officials or local tyrants and gentry, then it would be no different from attracting the Red bandits and inviting them to make a comeback. The reason why the Red bandits were able to invade these places in the past was because most people's lives were unstable, and they only saw a small number of people benefiting themselves at the expense of others and doing whatever they wanted, which created a feeling of injustice. Therefore, upon hearing theories such as class struggle, they felt that an opportunity to vent their anger had arrived and spontaneously followed. Now, we must correct this habit and give the masses a hope of a government of the people, by the people, and for the people, as well as a way to achieve this hope. What is the method? The late Premier Sun Yat-sen's instructions on how to start implementing local autonomy have already enlightened us: (1) Clear household registration, (2) Establish agencies, (3) Determine land prices, (4) Repair roads, (5) Reclaim wasteland, (6) Run schools. The method of clearing household registration is to ensure that, in addition to a small number of people who exclusively enjoy rights, all others who do not fulfill their obligations cannot enjoy rights, so there will be no shortage of people willing to undertake the task of autonomy. Establishing agencies means that the Food Administration Bureau is the most important, and other agencies for the production and manufacturing of clothing, housing, and transportation needs should also be gradually established and managed to ensure that the people's livelihood needs are adjusted at any time to prevent shortages or imbalances. Determining land prices means that landowners should report their own prices, and the autonomous organizations should levy taxes based on the prices, and they can also buy land at the prices. The increase in land prices in the future will belong to the organization. In this way, landowners cannot sit back and enjoy unearned profits, and it will be easy to achieve the goal of land to the tiller in the future. Repairing roads means repairing them with the obligatory labor of the residents. With convenient transportation, civilization will also advance. Reclaiming wasteland should be divided into two types: public management and private cultivation. The construction work for the publicly managed land should also be done with obligatory labor. When the wasteland is reclaimed, the public and private income will be abundant. Running schools means giving all local children and adults the opportunity to receive free education, and the school's expenses should also be supplied with obligatory labor. These are all things that all localities in the country should do first, but no locality has done them yet, which is a real proof of the government's dereliction of duty. We who serve in the government should all take the blame. To make up for our mistakes, we should start by doing this in the newly recovered areas of Jiangxi because after these areas were occupied by the communists, the population fled, the land deeds were burned, and the agencies were destroyed, so they need to be reorganized from scratch. Cursory settlement and thorough reorganization require the same procedures, so why not use the thorough method? This time, the Commander-in-Chief personally led the expedition, not only with brave soldiers but also with many loyal comrades as members of the Jiangxi Party Affairs and Political Affairs Committee. I believe that all comrades will follow the Premier Sun Yat-sen's teachings and plan to start implementing local autonomy, and those of us who remain in the rear should also pay attention to how to gradually implement autonomy in all localities. If we can do this, the elimination of the communists will be thorough, and there will be no more battles like Jiangxi in the future. As for the two more important events recently, one is Shi You-san's rebellion. Shi You-san is fickle. This time, he took advantage of the fact that the Red bandits had not yet been eliminated and the Korean tragedy had occurred to raise troops and provoke conflict, which is hated by the people of the country. The government has already issued a clear order to suppress him, and it will be resolved soon. The other is the heavy rain causing disaster. Recently, Guangdong, Hebei, Henan, Hubei, and northern Jiangsu have been hit by floods, and even near the capital, there is a fear of a poor autumn harvest. This is due to the lack of forests and the disrepair of water conservancy, and fundamental relief measures must be planned, but temporary measures cannot be ignored. The government has ordered the disaster-stricken provinces to prepare for famine relief in advance to prevent problems before they occur. Funds have also been allocated to provide relief to the current disaster victims, which should alleviate the difficulties. The meeting adjourned after the speech.

Legislative Yuan Passes Bank Exchange Coupon Issuance Tax

▲ Ministry of Finance Has Already Scheduled Promulgation and Implementation Within Days

The draft law on bank exchange coupon issuance tax has been submitted by the Legislative Yuan and passed. The full text of the draft is as follows: (Article 1) Banks specially permitted by the National Government to issue exchange coupons shall pay exchange coupon issuance tax. (Article 2) Banks issuing exchange coupons shall maintain a full reserve, with 60% as cash reserve and 40% as guarantee reserve. (Article 3) Banks issuing exchange coupons shall provide the following information: (1) Bank name and location; (2) Types of exchange coupons (e.g., silver dollar coupons, subsidiary currency coupons, etc.); (3) Types and detailed amounts of reserves; (4) Total issuance amount for the most recent year. After the Ministry of Finance investigates and confirms the above items, it may issue an issuance tax investigation certificate, which shall be renewed annually without a fee. (Article 4) The issuance tax rate shall be 2% based on the amount of the guarantee reserve. The portion of the cash reserve shall be exempt from issuance tax. (Article 5) The issuance tax shall be collected annually at the beginning of each year. (Article 6) If the Ministry of Finance deems the information provided by the bank in accordance with Article 3 to be inaccurate, it may temporarily organize a review committee to assess it. The review committee shall be composed of one person each from the Ministry of Finance, the Auditing Department, the Bankers Association, and the Chamber of Commerce. (Article 7) If a bank fails to pay the exchange coupon issuance tax, the Ministry of Finance may revoke its special issuance right. (Article 8) The tax payable on the portion of exchange coupons used shall still be borne by the issuing bank; however, the issuing bank may recover the tax from the bank using the coupons. (Article 9) This tax law shall take effect from the date of promulgation.

Yesterday, a reporter from the Daily News visited Mr. Lin Kang-hou, a standing committee member of the Bankers Association, to inquire about the banknote tax. According to him, the total amount of banknotes and government bonds in China is 500 million yuan, with government bonds accounting for 200 million yuan, or 40%, and banknotes accounting for 300 million yuan, or 60%. According to Article 4 of the Exchange Coupon Issuance Tax Law, the government can collect 5 million yuan annually.

Minister Wang's Inspection of Pyongyang

▲ The Situation in the Korean Territory Has Not Fully Returned to Normal

An Dong dispatch: According to a visitor returning from Pyongyang, Korea, Minister Wang Rong-bao, the ambassador to Japan, accompanied by Consul Ren Jia-feng stationed in Kobe, arrived in Gyeongseong (Seoul), Korea, for inspection. After the inspection concluded, he took a route westward to inspect. He originally planned to arrive in Pyongyang by train on the evening of the 16th, but it was temporarily postponed for one night. He arrived at Pyongyang Station at 7:17 AM on the 17th. Minister Wang was accompanied by five people, including Consul General Zhang Wei-cheng of Gyeongseong and Consul Ren Jia-feng of Kobe. Members of the Pyongyang Consulate and Meng Xian-shi, Chairman of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce, stood on the platform to welcome him. After Wang got off the train, he greeted the welcomers and then took automobiles to the Pyongyang Hotel. After a light refreshment and a short rest, he took an automobile to the refugee camp. After inspecting for a week, he gave a speech to comfort the refugees. At this time, the refugees cried bitterly, and their voices shook the roof. They all demanded a solution for relief. Wang left the refugee camp and went to the public cemetery. All that could be seen were mounds of yellow earth, and the graves were piled upon each other. According to Chinese compatriots who witnessed it, more than 400 Chinese compatriots were killed in this incident. During the riots on the 4th and 5th, Chinese corpses were everywhere along the streets. The Japanese police dug more than 90 pits in the public cemetery outside the city, and each pit buried four or five corpses. The exact number of wounded and dead is unknown. The Japanese are trying to cover up, saying that there is no such number. Minister Wang will report the actual situation of the investigation to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs at any time. He stayed overnight at the Pyongyang Hotel, and the Japanese side sent police to protect him. On the morning of the 18th, he took a train from Pyongyang to Incheon. In the afternoon of the same day, at 2:00 PM, he returned to Pyongyang. At 5:00 PM on the 19th, he boarded the train eastward to Gyeongseong. He is scheduled to go to Sinuiju on the 22nd for an on-site inspection, and then cross the Yalu River westward and take the Anfeng Line to return home.

On the way to the country, there are more than 700 or 800 unemployed Chinese in Pyongyang, with their livelihoods cut off. They are now being sent back to their country by the Pyongyang Chinese Chamber of Commerce to seek other livelihoods.

Another report: At 10:00 AM on the 20th, more than 60 Korean rioters suddenly appeared in Sinuiju, across the river from this city, each holding stones, intending to riot again. They threw several stones at the gate of the Xin'yan Iron Factory and completely smashed the glass windows of Fu Fengtai, and then fled. At 2:00 PM on the 21st, the Japanese authorities in Sinuiju specially summoned representatives from all sectors of Chinese and Japanese merchants to hold a plenary meeting to discuss future protection methods. It can be seen that the situation in various parts of the Korean territory has not completely returned to a state of peace. (21st)

The Severity of the Flood in the Capital

▲ The Water Reaches Chest Level in the Area of the Central Party Headquarters on Huangpu Road

▲ Various Agencies Have Already Discussed Emergency Relief and Rescue Measures

▲ The Flood is Due to Continuous Rain and Flash Floods from the Upper Reaches

Beijing Dispatch: The continuous rain has caused the water level in the north and south of the city and in Xiaguan to rise day by day. The crucial road surfaces in Xiaguan have been completely washed away. The water is knee-deep from Zhongshan Wharf to Yijiang Gate. In the area of the Three Archway Huangpu Road of the Central Party Headquarters, the water has reached chest level. On both sides of the Qinhuai River in the south of the city, in places like Dashiba Street and Confucius Temple, the water has already entered the houses. Although it cleared up on the 25th, the floodwater has not receded at all. This is because the river water and the river water are at the same level. It is not easy to leave unless the river tide ebbs. Therefore, the 10,000+ population in more than 4,100 households in the area from outside the Hailin Gate in Xiaguan to the Commercial Bureau Street still moved the submerged furniture and utensils to the side of the Commercial Bureau Street in the morning of the 26th. They were exposed to the sky, the smoke and fire were interrupted, the weak were crying with hunger, and the old and strong were sobbing. The situation was extremely miserable. Therefore, the National Government, the Municipal Government, and the Police Department are paying close attention to this and have convened meetings to discuss relief plans. The findings of the investigation are briefly described below.

▲ Forming an Emergency Relief Association The Executive Yuan recently received an order from the National Government to allocate three yuan to relieve the flood in the capital. It ordered the Ministry of Interior to convene relevant agencies in the capital to properly handle relief matters. After receiving the order, the Ministry of Interior notified the agencies on the morning of the 25th and held a meeting at the Ministry of Interior at 3:00 PM that afternoon. The representatives attending were Li Fan-guo and Chen Rui from the Executive Yuan, Zhang Wo-hua, Wang Ting-feng-yang, Chen Feng-zhang, Zhu Jiu-ying, and Zhang Fu-bao from the Ministry of Interior, Zhang Fu-heng and Wang Fu-heng from the Beijing Municipal Government, Hong from the Relief Committee, Xie Guan-yi from the Capital Police Department, and Li Jie-cai from the Municipal Social Bureau. Zhang Wo-hua was elected as the chairman. The following resolutions were made: (1) To organize the Capital Flood Emergency Relief Committee, divided into four groups: General Affairs, Relief, Investigation, and Fundraising. Zhang Wo-hua was elected as the chairman and Chen Rui as the vice chairman, and seventeen people were elected as members. (2) To nominate Wang Ting-yang to draft the regulations of the association. (3) To set the time to gather at the Ministry of Interior at 8:00 AM on the 26th to go to the following areas to investigate the flood: Xiaguan: Chen Rui, Chen Feng-zhang; Pukou: Li Jie-cai, Xie Guan-yi; Tongji Gate, Qinhuai River area: Wang Ting-yang, Hong ; Shuixi Gate: Zhu Jiu-ying, Zhang . Also, at 1:00 PM on the 26th, the second meeting was held at the Ministry of Interior. First, the regulations of the Emergency Relief Association were discussed. After being revised and passed item by item, the chairman announced the official establishment of the Flood Emergency Relief Association, which was scheduled to officially start work immediately. Then, the discussion focused on investigating the disaster situation in various places, and obtaining funds from the Ministry of Finance for relief, etc. The meeting adjourned at about 5:00 PM.

▲ Municipal Government Meeting At 1:00 PM on the 25th, Mayor Wei Dao-ming, Secretary-General Ma Shou-hua, Director of the Social Bureau Li Jie-cai, Director of the Public Works Bureau Ma Yi-qun, Director of the Health Bureau Mei Yi-lin, and others held a temporary emergency meeting at the Municipal Government to decide on three measures to address the flood relief issue: (1) Prevention and dredging: The Public Works Bureau will send workers to block the river water and lake water to prevent flooding. At the same time, they will try to drain the water from various places in the city and select high places inside and outside the city to build thatched sheds to accommodate the victims to avoid displacement. (2) Relief: The Social Bureau will convene various groups to find ways to relieve the victims to save the lives of all people. (3) Rescue: The Health Bureau will send personnel to diagnose and treat diseases for the victims and inject preventive vaccines to prevent epidemics after the disaster.

▲ Causes of the Flood Ma Yi-qun, Director of the Beijing Municipal Public Works Bureau, issued a statement on the flood on the 25th. According to him, "I (Ma said himself) led the engineering team to inspect the flood situation in various parts of the city at dawn this morning and gave instructions on rescue methods. The cause of this flood is due to the continuous cloudy rain and the flash floods from the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. The water level of the Yangtze River has been one or two feet higher than the land. Therefore, it is increasingly out of control. Now, in addition to trying to block the water, dredging and guiding have become ineffective. Fortunately, the weather has cleared today. If there is no more rain in the area along the Yangtze River within three to five days, the water level of the Yangtze River will drop, and the floodwater in the city will be easily drained. Now the sandbags placed on the river bank in Xiaguan have also been completely submerged by the rising river water, and the flooded shanties have nowhere to go. This bureau has built dozens of large thatched sheds on the open space of Longchi Nunnery to accommodate the victims and will continue to select land inside and outside the city to build sheds to avoid displacement. The previously dug open ditches near Sajiawan in the north of the city are still beneficial for drainage and should not be a problem. The New Vegetable Market and its surroundings have always used Xiliuwan as the main channel for water discharge. However, the mountain water is coming too quickly, and the old river channels from Xiliuwan to Xiqiao, Taiping Bridge, and Jinchuan Gate are narrow and winding, which slows down the water discharge. Now we are trying to make it flow smoothly and guide it into the low-lying open space for storage. The water is five or six feet deep in the Huangpu Road area, and traffic is completely cut off. This is due to the intrusion of lake water. We are now planning to block it to prevent it from continuing to rise and send a large number of engineering teams to use machines to pump water and maintain traffic. As for the south of the city, on both sides of the Qinhuai River, thousands of sandbags had already been placed the night before, but due to the heavy rain and the backflow of the river water, the river water overturned the sandbags in an instant and flowed into the houses on both sides, making the previous defense work equal to zero. Today the weather is clear, and the water has gradually flowed out from Xiguan. The riverbed may be exposed within a day or two. We are now continuing to fill the important riverbanks with sandbags to prevent flooding."

The Jinghu Railway After the Heavy Rain

▲ The Earth Wall of Yangpeng Mountain Collapsed

▲ The Entrance of the Tunnel is Filled with Yellow Mud

▲ Consequently, Traffic is Blocked

The Shanghai-Nanjing Railway's afternoon express train passed Zhenjiang at 3 PM the day before yesterday, but the water was deep at the entrance of the tunnel. Unexpectedly, heavy rain poured down from 4 to 5 PM. The special express train departing from Nanjing was washed away by the water below Yaohuamen first, and then submerged. The gravel under the sleepers was empty, and there was a fear of a train sinking. At the same time, the slopes on both sides of the Zhenjiang tunnel, about tens of feet high, were all yellow earth without stone masonry. The rainwater was powerful and pressed the earth down, and the floating earth piled up on the rails to more than ten feet. The water between the slopes was six or seven feet deep. Traffic was immediately cut off. The special express train then turned back to Nanjing. The trains from Shanghai to Zhenjiang could have dropped off passengers under the Heiqiao near the tunnel, but unexpectedly at about 8 PM, the wall of Yangpeng Mountain, less than half a mile from the tunnel, about ten feet high, collapsed onto the track with a loud bang. The soil piled up to a height of thirty feet, covering an area of about several acres. Three power poles were also broken. Therefore, the northbound train could only stop at the Nanmen Station. The train from Wuxi to Zhenjiang on the 25th ran as usual and returned to Nanmen. The station has no two-way tracks and no road sign to the station. After the passengers got on and off, it only drove in reverse. After reaching Zazhe, the train head could be transferred to the front of the train, but it was still the coal car in front and the chimney in the back, still driving in reverse. As for Nanmen Station, there has always been a small road leading to Nanmen. From Zhongzheng Road directly to the station, there is an 18-meter-wide avenue that can allow cars to pass smoothly. Therefore, although the trains could not reach the main station yesterday, the traffic was not difficult. As for the area between Nanjing and Zhenjiang, because the flood at Yaohuamen has not receded and the water is several feet deep at the Qiaotou Station, the trains dare not run. Northbound train tickets are sold to Zhenjiang. Those who want to go to Nanjing must either take a small wheel or a large upstream wheel. Those who want to go to Jiangbei can only hire sailboats because the cars are not running. Most of the travelers going west and north are temporarily staying in Zhenjiang inns. According to a reporter's investigation, the soil in the tunnel and Yangpeng Mountain can be removed and repaired tonight. The Nanjing-Zhenjiang section can be opened to traffic this afternoon, and the entire line can be restored to its original condition at the latest tomorrow. The Zhenjiang tunnel has not been repaired for many years. The left and right slopes on both sides of the tunnel entrance should be entirely built with stone blocks, and cement should be added to the slope walls.

Clear outlet ditches, so that mountain water has a way out and has the power to resist soil swelling. If this can be done, even if there is heavy rain, the soil will not collapse and fill the track, cutting off traffic. The road should quickly seek remedial measures. (26th)

Wuhu Suffers Major Flood Disaster

▲ The Entire City is Submerged and All Businesses are Closed

▲ Dikes Collapse and 200,000 Mu of Fields are Flooded

Wuhu dispatch: The water level in Wuhu has been gradually rising since the beginning of summer. At first, it was thought to be due to seasonal factors, but unexpectedly heavy rain poured down all day, lasting for almost two weeks, so that the water level increased unabated. Until the recent two days, the river water rose sharply, the tide flowed back, and the inland river rushed down due to torrential mountain floods, like pouring water from a high place. The entire city of Wuhu is now like an island in the center. The core areas, such as Dama Road, Erjie, Changjie, and Doumen Alley, are all submerged, reaching a depth of more than two feet. Even rickshaws are at risk of floating. All businesses and shops are closed. The avenues where cars and horses used to gallop are now areas where rafts and basins wander, and the scene is extremely tragic. Areas such as Dongmen and Jinmamen are slightly lower in elevation, and the water depth has reached more than seven feet. The Nanchengmen is completely submerged. The Public Security Bureau has prohibited pedestrians from traveling to avoid drowning. The houses along the Merchants' Wharf along the river only have a foot or so exposed above the water. Most of the residents have moved to higher ground to build sheds for shelter. In addition to the Wanzi Society, which has already raised 2,000 thousand copper coins for distribution, officials, gentry, and all sectors are now continuing to seek ways to provide relief. The disaster is even more severe in the villages and polder fields. Wuhu is a rice-producing area, with a total of more than 400,000 mu of farmland. After the flood broke out, County Magistrate Yu Yu-ying led various polder affairs bureaus to go to the villages to carry out rescue work every day. Therefore, only small polders such as Baotai and Dingba collapsed. Unexpectedly, the Shangfenglin and Xiafenglin polders, the first polders in the southern countryside of Wuyi, suddenly collapsed for more than five feet last night. In addition to using civilian boats and sacks to block and rescue, the villagers immediately beat gongs and rushed to the county government to report the alarm. County Magistrate Yu rushed to supervise the rescue overnight. The real reason was that the rain was heavy and the wind was strong, and it was impossible to recover. The collapse continued until 3:00 AM this morning. The rescuers were almost killed by the flood. Unexpectedly, by 3:00 PM today, the river tide had increased again, and the water level suddenly increased by more than two feet, causing the Mapu polder, which is adjacent to the Fenglin polder, to overflow and become unrecoverable by 3:00 PM this afternoon. It is estimated that a total of about 170,000 to 180,000 mu of fertile land has been submerged, and the deaths and losses of livestock and houses are even more difficult to count. Until the time of publication, it is still raining heavily, and the water level is still increasing every hour. People are panicked and cannot live in peace. The telegram from Wuhu County Magistrate Yu Yu-ying to Chairman Chen of the Provincial Government is recorded below: (Privately, because the situation of the Fenglin polder was critical, the county magistrate has already reported in detail in the Yang Jing telegrams. The county magistrate rushed to the polder with the team at the second watch of the night of July 23 to supervise the polder directors and polder chiefs to do their best to rescue. The reported dangerous places have already been turned from danger to safety. However, last night's heavy rain continued with strong winds all night. Mountain floods broke out and the river tide flowed backwards, rushing straight down, like pouring water from a high place. The water surface was more than a foot higher than the polder embankment, and the added child embankment also collapsed, causing the place where the polder was close to Tiancheng Lake to be flooded at 3:00 AM on the night of July 23. The rescue was not effective until 8:00 AM on the 24th, causing it to collapse. Fenglin and Mapu are only separated by a dike. Now we are moving all our efforts to protect Mapu (reporter's note: Mapu has collapsed after this telegram was sent). However, the sky is not clear and the wind does not stop, and I am deeply anxious. In addition to reporting the details at any time, I respectfully report it. Wuhu County Magistrate Yu) (24th)

Tao Dunli Escapes in Shenyang

▲ The Military Law Office Orders Strict Apprehension

▲ The Warden of the Detention Center Has Been Detained

Shenyang dispatch: Mr. Tao Dunli, who was arrested in Beidaihe last autumn for plotting a mutiny, has been handed over to the Military Law Office for interrogation since he was escorted to Shenyang. He has not yet been sentenced and is being held in the detention center of the First Prison. The treatment is very generous. Last month, Tao asked someone to intercede for him due to illness. With the permission of the Military Law authorities, he can go out to the Japanese-run Red Cross Hospital for diagnosis and treatment every day. A certain Yang is sent by the detention center to accompany him in and out to monitor his actions. Tao often goes to his residence in Zhonghua Lane, Wuwei Road, in the commercial district, in addition to going to the hospital, but still returns to the detention center every night to stay. This has been going on for a month, and many people do not suspect that he has anything else. Unexpectedly, Tao went out as usual on the afternoon of the 20th of this month and did not return until night. At about 11:00 PM, the detention center sent someone to visit Tao's residence. They found the doors were tightly closed and the place was empty. A certain Yang, who was monitoring Tao, also disappeared at the same time. It is not known whether he escaped with him or was murdered. At this point, the detention center could do nothing but report the situation to the Military Law Office. Director Lei of the Military Law Office was furious when he heard the news. He immediately informed the military and police agencies to investigate and apprehend strictly. On the one hand, he believed that Warden Yang Yu-nan of the detention center had been indulgent on weekdays and did not exercise caution, allowing him to escape. He then detained Yang and waited for Tao to be arrested before punishing him. However, there is still no news as of today. It is said that Tao's escape this time is related to the current situation. (July 22)

Guangdong Issues 30 Million Customs Treasury Bonds

Guangdong dispatch: The Guangdong Province has issued 30 million yuan of customs-backed lottery treasury bonds. The issuance regulations have been passed. The contents are as follows: the total amount of lottery bonds is 30 million yuan, divided into 3 million tickets, with a face value of ten yuan per ticket. Each ticket is divided into ten strips and is scheduled to be issued starting from August of this year. The customs revenue of Guangdong and Guangxi is used as collateral. Starting from August 16, 500,000 yuan will be allocated every half month and handed over to the bank or silver house designated by the Treasury Bond Fund Management Committee for safekeeping, in order to provide lottery prizes and repay principal and interest. The treasury bond is set at an annual interest rate of 8%. August 1st of each year is the interest payment period. A lottery method is used every month to draw 100,000 tickets. The prizes and principal repayment are awarded according to the following grades: one first prize, with a prize of 150,000 silver dollars per ticket; one second prize, with a prize of 20,000 silver dollars per ticket; one third prize, with a prize of 10,000 silver dollars per ticket; one fourth prize, with a prize of 20 silver dollars per ticket. All other tickets will only have their principal of seven yuan repaid. The treasury bonds drawn in the previous item will not pay interest. October 15, 1931, will be the first lottery date, and a lottery will be held once a month thereafter on the 15th of each month. All lottery repayments of principal and interest will be handled by the Treasury Bond Fund Management Committee. This treasury bond is in bearer form and can be freely bought, sold, mortgaged, and used as collateral for public service deposits. (July 23)

Local Correspondence

Nanhui

The County Government Secretary's Wife Died from Suicide The wife of Xiong Yu-wu, the secretary of this county's government, lived with her husband in the county government's inner chamber. The relationship between the couple was very good on weekdays, but there have been some quarrels recently. Unexpectedly, Mrs. Xiong suddenly hanged herself from the bedpost in the middle of the night yesterday while Xiong was sound asleep. Xiong only discovered it at dawn, but it was too late to save her.

Three Agencies Compete for the Yimiao Land The Chenghuang Temple used to have more than 400 mu of temple land, but it has been encroached upon by people throughout history. Now, the public First Hospital advocates that the rental income of the temple land should be used as the hospital's fund. At the same time, the First District Office advocates holding a funeral home to accommodate exposed corpses. And the managers of the temple also organized a temple property management committee to use the annual rental income to run charitable undertakings. The three parties are fiercely competing and refusing to give in, making it impossible for the county government to resolve the issue.

Suzhou

The County Government Reports the Disaster Situation The continuous rain for many days has turned the rural areas into a swamp. The sounds of collapsing houses and the overflowing water in the urban areas are endless. More than a dozen sections of the city wall have also collapsed. Farmers from various villages have been reporting to the county government for relief, and there have been several cases of requests to send personnel to inspect the damage every day. On the 27th, the county government specially telegraphed the Department of Finance and the Department of Civil Affairs, saying that the county has been experiencing continuous heavy rain day and night, and the low-lying fields have all become swamps. The seedlings have all been submerged. According to reports from the county farmers' association and various district chiefs, the matter concerns the people's food supply and should be addressed urgently. In addition to ordering the agricultural improvement field to guide remediation, we are drafting methods to follow in the hope of salvaging the autumn harvest. We are also reporting separately, and we are telegraphing to report.

The Lawyer's Wife Petitions for Reconsideration Jiang, the wife of Shanghai lawyer Ren Zhen-nan, filed a case against Ren Zhen-nan for pederasty. The Shanghai court gave an acquittal. Ren Jiang was dissatisfied and appealed to the High Court to petition for reconsideration.

Robbery and Injury at Huoshao Bridge Near Huoshao Bridge outside Xumen, in Zhang's house in the 21st Tu of the 11th Du, at about 2:00 AM on the 27th, seven robbers wearing gray short clothes suddenly came to rob the house, overturned boxes and cabinets, and robbed gold and silver jewelry, cash, and clothing worth about 700 yuan. Four victims were injured. They fired two shots before leaving. Afterwards, the victims reported the incident to the relevant branch office to pursue the robbers. Because the Public Security Bureau said that the area was close to the downtown area and not far from the Taihu bandit suppression headquarters, they ordered strict searches to catch the robbers and bring them to justice.

Songjiang

Preparing for Township Elections in the First District: This county's districts have received orders to hold elections for township chiefs, deputy chiefs, and supervisory committee members. Some districts have already submitted reports of completion, while others are still in preparation. It is learned that the First District Office will discuss the election matters of township chiefs, deputy chiefs, and supervisory committee members at the 22nd District Affairs Meeting today (27th). It was resolved that the list of candidates will be announced immediately after approval. If any omissions are found during the announcement period, the person concerned may report corrections. The election period for each township will be from the 16th to the end of the month.

Communist Cao Shuming Sent Back for Retrial: Cao Shuming, a communist captured in Fengjing by the county government, was previously submitted to the High Court for trial as a reactionary. Now, the High Court believes that the facts of the crime and evidence of the said offender need to be sent back for retrial, and orders the county government to comply. Magistrate Shen specially dispatched administrative police officer Dong Futang to Suzhou to bring Cao Shuming back to Songjiang on the 27th, to be detained for retrial and investigation.

New Prison Warden Takes Office: Zheng Ligeng, the prison warden of this county, was ordered by the High Court to be transferred with Li Yurui, the prison warden of Danyang County. Mr. Li has now completed his duties in Danyang and arrived in Songjiang today. He is scheduled to take office on the 28th.

Wuxi

Settlement of Compensation for the Li Ashou Tragedy: Li Ashou, a carpenter at the Yeqin Silk Factory outside the East Gate, died tragically due to a conflict with the gate guard of the Yongyu Factory while delivering food. In addition to the family filing a lawsuit with the County Court to punish the perpetrators, a support association was organized by various labor unions to handle the matter fully and offer rewards for the arrest of Wu Xilin and Zhu Meisen, employees of the Yongyu Silk Factory. Although the Yongyu Silk Factory repeatedly approached the support association to negotiate compensation for the family, no results were achieved. Recently, the Yongyu Silk Factory and Wu Xilin and Zhu Meisen commissioned Hua Mengyu as their full representative to discuss the compensation issue with the family and engaged Hu Nianqian and Li Tiping as witnesses. After receiving a report from the family, Li Bao’s, the support association immediately held an emergency meeting and decided that Li Bao’s, the family, should formally negotiate with Hua Mengyu, the full representative of the Yongyu Silk Factory and Wu and Zhu. As a result, regarding the compensation issue for the tragic death of Li Ashou, the Yongyu Silk Factory agreed to allocate 4,400 yuan. In addition, the issue of punishing the perpetrators will be handled by the County Court. After the decision was made, Hua Mengyu, Hu Nianqian, Li Tiping, Li Bao’s the family, Wang Zhaodi, and all members of the support association inspected and delivered the compensation clearly yesterday. Thus, the long-unresolved compensation issue for the tragic case has been resolved.

Third District Chief Accused: Zou Qingxiang, the chief of the Third District of the county, has been in office for more than a year and has not accomplished anything in district administration. Recently, Yuan Zizhi, Hui Guolan, Jiang Bingzhi, and other residents of the district listed his wrongdoings and filed accusations with the county government and the Department of Civil Affairs, requesting that personnel be sent immediately to thoroughly investigate and dismiss him from office.

Various Industries Organize Japanese Goods Inspection Teams: Since the Wanbaoshan incident involving Koreans, the people of the whole country have been deeply indignant. All sectors of Wuxi have organized an Anti-Japanese Aid-to-Overseas-Chinese Committee to actively carry out anti-Japanese work. Yesterday, fourteen industries, including silk and cloth, northern goods, mountain goods, foreign goods, hardware, dyeing and weaving, yarn shops, hosiery, coal, paper, books, printing, Western medicine, and transportation, resolved at the County Chamber of Commerce to automatically oppose Japan in accordance with the County Chamber of Commerce's announcement. Inspection teams will be organized immediately to register Japanese goods, and the handling situation has been reported to the County Party Department.

Provincial Order Strictly Prohibits Export of Rice: Continuous rain for days has turned Jiangsu Province into a disaster area. Rice prices are gradually soaring due to a lack of sources. The county government yesterday received instructions from the provincial government to strictly prohibit the export of rice from the province to maintain the people's food supply. Magistrate Chen, upon receiving the order, has forwarded it to the County Chamber of Commerce and the Rice Grain Guild for notification.

Jiangyin

Business Tax Amounting to 24,000 Yuan: The amount of business tax in Jiangyin was previously determined by various industry meetings to be 20,000 yuan for the entire county throughout the year. Subsequently, instructions were received from the Finance Department that the amount was too far off the ratio. Wu Shuying, chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, accompanied Shen, director of the Finance Bureau, to the provincial department to negotiate. The Finance Department required a settlement of 27,000 yuan based on 45% of the quota. After Chairman Wu repeatedly stated the difficult situation of commercial decline, the amount was increased to 24,000 yuan to be handled by the Chamber of Commerce. Both parties signed a contract. After returning to Cheng, the collection began from various industries.

Changzhou

Assault on Police Occurs in the Northern Suburbs: The Recruitment Office of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force of the Capital established a recruitment office in Wuyi. On the 25th, recruitment officers Ma Zhian and others went to Xiaomaojia Village in Daguigou, a village in the northern suburbs, to recruit, which led to a conflict with the villagers. Recruitment Officer Ma immediately reported to the Third Substation of the First Public Security Bureau in charge and requested police assistance. On the morning of the 26th, police officers Ding Kunbao and Wang Guoliang were dispatched to assist the recruitment officers in investigating the incident. However, upon arriving at the village, a villager, Wu Liangsheng, immediately fought with the police officers, and Jin Bosheng came out and beat a gong, causing nearby villagers to gather and the order to be in chaos. Unscrupulous elements even threw police officer Wang Guoliang into the river. Fortunately, Wang desperately climbed ashore and no one died, but all the police officers were seriously injured. The Third Substation received the report and dispatched more police to rescue them and arrested the criminals Wu Liangsheng and others, who were sent to the Public Security Bureau in the city for interrogation.

Xie Shaoqing Sentenced to Four Years in Prison for Rape: The District Court accepted the case of Xie Shaoqing raping Chen Ruiying. Yesterday morning, Judge Yang Changdi of the Criminal Court came to the court at 10 o'clock to interrogate Xie Shaoqing after summoning him. He was immediately sentenced to four years of imprisonment. The number of days in custody before the verdict was reached was offset by two days for one day of imprisonment. After the sentence was announced, he was ordered to be returned to custody to await the determination period before being sent to prison for execution.

Mutiny of the Tanggou Township Militia: The militia of Tangjiagou Township in the Yudong District of Nantong were all temporarily recruited. The districts are now blocking the escape routes.

Court Prepares for Upgrade: The Ministry of Judicial Administration believes that the number of civil and criminal appeals in the counties of Nantong, Rugao, Taixing, Dongtai, and Haimen in Jiangbei is increasing daily. For the convenience of the parties concerned, the Nantong County Court will be upgraded and expanded into a District Court. The court is preparing to proceed.

Revenge Killing Case Occurs in Yiyu: A revenge killing case occurred in Yiyu District in the eastern countryside. The deceased, Jiang Defei, was the surrendered bandit leader. The death was extremely tragic. The family has reported the case and is seeking the arrest of the murderer.

Water Diversion Dispute Resolved by the Judiciary: The heavy rain in Nantong has caused a disaster. Sanyu and Yuxi had a conflict of interest over water diversion between the upstream and downstream areas, resulting in a major fight. The security regiment also joined in, causing more than 20 rural farmers to be injured and killed. The dispute between the two sides is very fierce and they have filed lawsuits in court. The trial is scheduled for the 27th.

Continuous Rain and More Severe Disaster: Continuous rain in Tongyi has turned the four rural areas into swamps. Land and water transportation are completely cut off. Recently, the water depth in the countryside has reached more than seven feet, and houses are already in the water. The harvest of cotton and beans is hopeless.

Yangzhou

Business Tax Approved to be Handled by Businesses: The Business Tax Bureau of this county was established more than four months ago. Although Ding Buzhou was appointed as the director by the Finance Department and ordered all businesses to register, there was still no way to collect the tax. Subsequently, the Chamber of Commerce repeatedly convened the chambers of commerce in the four rural areas and various trade associations to discuss changing it to a contracted system. It has now been approved by the Finance Department that the annual contracted amount for Jiangdu is 45,000 yuan. It is heard that the Finance Department believes that since the tax is contracted by the businesses, there is no need to set up a bureau, and Director Ding will be reassigned as a collection supervisor to assist.

Gaoyou

Bao Ying County Magistrate Accused of Thorough Investigation: The magistrate of Bao Ying County was recently accused by Wang Zhuren and Li Shuzhen, citizens of the county, of numerous misdeeds in the provincial government. The provincial government has now ordered the Department of Civil Affairs to instruct County Magistrate Wang of this county to conduct a thorough investigation and report the facts to be used for verification.

Kidnapping Case Occurs in Zhao Jiahe: The family of a farmer surnamed Xiang in Zhaojiahe, the tenth district of the county, was suddenly visited by more than ten bandits armed with guns the night before last. After searching and robbing, they kidnapped his young son. Then they went to the Zhang family next door, ransacked the boxes and cabinets, and robbed clothing, silver dollars, and other items worth more than a hundred yuan. Before leaving, they also kidnapped Zhang's young son and instructed the two families to prepare 7,000 yuan each within ten days to redeem them.

Water News from This County: The water level of the canal in this county reached one zhang six chi three cun at the Royal Wharf today (25th). Sun Zhehong, Director of the Department of Construction, specially accompanied the Provincial Committee to inspect the water level by mail. It is heard that Director Sun is considering the agricultural products of the lower river area and advocates not opening the dam for the time being. However, the farmers in the west of the lake, because the water level there is very high, specially sent a large number of representatives to request the opening of the dam, while the farmers in the lower river area, because opening the dam means that there is no hope for agricultural production, have also sent representatives to the city to protect the dam.

Hefei

Details of the Crackdown on Bone-Stealing Organizations: Here, the incidents of demons stealing bones are not only getting worse, but also the cases of women and children in the four rural areas being drugged, having their breasts and genitals cut off, and then being covered with plasters, and dying when the plasters are removed, are too numerous to mention. As a result, the villagers guard their wives during the day and watch over their ancestral graves at night, almost causing the entire territory to be disturbed. After County Magistrate Zhang Shusen, the town and township security associations, and others offered rewards for the arrest, on the 17th, someone reported to the Public Security Bureau that this organization was located inside Lu Shao Ting’s market house south of Xiao Dong Men (Small East Gate). Director Xu Chun immediately joined forces with Wang Jifu of the Dongwai Water Patrol Bureau and led the police to arrest them. After inquiring in the vicinity, it was learned that four people had escaped beforehand. Bureau Officer Wang guarded the two city gates of Da Dong (Big East) and Xiao Dong, and Director Xu immediately entered to search and arrest. Only Dan Guo's, her son-in-law Zu Muheng, and a young woman were found. However, many monk and Taoist robes, Guigu, Chisongzi, and talismans, many broken small coffin boards, and 1,200 yuan in paper money were found. Just as the interrogation was underway, Bureau Officer Wang intercepted an old Taoist, Hu Youzhi, 68 years old from Shandong, at Xiao Dong Men, and found bottles of hypnotic drugs, small knives, small scissors, steel needles, silver needles, and various talismans, and brought him to the bureau along with Dan Guo's and Zu Muheng for a brief interrogation.

They were immediately transferred to the county government. Due to the seriousness of the case, a secret interrogation is now underway. However, local public organizations, believing that this matter is related to the security of the entire county, have petitioned the 46th Division Headquarters and the county government to impose extreme penalties and to strictly arrest the accomplices and bring them to justice for interrogation.

Hechao Executed Robbers of Motor Vehicles by Firing Squad: The 46th Division Headquarters previously arrested Chen Shoujin and Liu Shifang, bandits who plotted to rob a Hechao motor vehicle. Chen was sentenced to death and Liu to 12 years of imprisonment after trial. Yesterday, Chen was taken out for execution by firing squad. Education News

Important News

Ministry of Education Plans to Draft Organizational Law for Primary and Secondary Schools

In order to actively rectify primary and secondary school education, the Ministry of Education, in addition to formulating primary and secondary school curriculum standards that will be promulgated soon, will subsequently compile equipment standards for primary and secondary schools, so that both educational administration and school management have a basis. In addition, regarding the organizational law of primary and secondary schools, because there has been no fixed standard in the past, the organizational system of schools in various places often changes with the preferences of the school administrative authorities, or when personnel changes, which greatly hinders the progress of education. The Ministry of Education, seeing this, is now drafting organizational laws for middle schools, and it is heard that the draft has been completed. After being revised and passed by the Ministry Affairs Meeting, it will be sent to the Legislative Yuan for review so that it can be formally promulgated.

League of Nations Plans to Send Personnel to China to Study Our Educational System

Reuter's Geneva, 26th: The League of Nations Committee on Intellectual Cooperation has now closed. At today's meeting, it repeatedly stated its willingness to provide China with the greatest possible assistance and send personnel to China to study the Chinese educational system.

Results of Re-election of Directors and Councilors of the Vocational Education Society Announced

The term of office for directors of the Chinese Vocational Education Society is four years, and half are re-elected every two years. The term of office for councilors is two years, and half are re-elected every year. The re-election of both directors and councilors was held simultaneously this year. Yesterday (26th) at 9:00 am, the votes were counted publicly at the society, supervised by Huang Renzhi, Shen Xinqing, and Wang Zhixin. A total of 51 votes were received for directors. As a result, Mu Jiechu received 23 votes, Shen Xinqing received 21 votes, Shi Liangcai received 19 votes, and Chen Guangfu received 17 votes. The above four were elected as directors. A total of 1,012 votes were received for councilors. As a result, Wang Yunwu received 826 votes, Chen Bulei received 672 votes, Pan Xulun received 592 votes,

Zou Bingwen received 559 votes, and Gao Jiansi received 511 votes. The above five were elected as councilors.
