Paris Celebrates Fifth Consecutive Victory

France Retains the Davis Cup

丨Defeats Great Britain Three to Two丨

▲Decisive Final Match丨Cochet of France Defeats Gregory of Britain▲

▲Gregory Initially Takes the Lead丨Unable to Sustain Advantage and Loses▲

Paris, 26th – France continues its fifth year of victory in the world tennis Davis Cup. In the final decisive singles match, Cochet of France defeated Gregory of Britain 6-4, 1-6, 9-7, 6-3. The overall match results were France 3, Great Britain 2.

Complete Match Results

Cochet (France) (3-6, 10-9, 6-2, 6-4) Austin (Great Britain)

Gregory (Great Britain) (4-6, 10-8, 6-0, 4-6, 6-4) Borotra (France)

Cochet and Brugnon (France) (6-1, 5-7, 6-3, 8-6) Hughes and Kingsley (Great Britain)

Austin (Great Britain) (7-5, 6-3, 3-6, 7-5) Borotra (France)

Cochet (France) (6-4, 1-6, 9-7, 6-3) Gregory (Great Britain)

▲Past Davis Cup Winners

The Davis Cup world tennis tournament began in 1900. To date, it has been held for thirty-one years. It was suspended for four years during the European War. Listed below are the winners of each edition:

1900丨1902 United States

1903丨1906 Great Britain

1907—1911 Australasia

1912 Great Britain

1913 United States

1914 Australasia

1915—1918 European War (No Tournament)

1919 Australasia

1920—1926 United States

1927—1931 France

Total

France 5 times United States 11 times

Great Britain 5 times Australasia 7 times

▲14,000 Spectators Watch in the Rain

During the match between Austin and Borotra, a light drizzle fell. As Cochet and Gregory entered the court, the rain intensified. Whether such a final match should be held was a question. However, the crowd clamored, and the players had no choice but to comply reluctantly. In reality, the court was slippery, and finding a firm foothold was extremely difficult. Later, the spectators watched in the rain, their cheers and shouts so enthusiastic that they completely forgot they were in a storm. There were about 14,000 spectators.

▲Gregory's Initial Lead and Subsequent Loss Regrettable

Gregory's loss to Cochet is extremely regrettable. Having gained the upper hand, he ultimately failed. This was the case in both the first and third sets. In the first set, Gregory led 4-1 but then lost five consecutive games, losing the set 4-6. In the second set, Gregory again took a four-game lead before Cochet won a single game, with Gregory winning decisively 6-1. In the third set, Gregory again led 5-2, but unexpectedly failed, and the set extended to sixteen games, with Cochet winning. In the fourth set, Cochet fully displayed his talent and won effortlessly. It was his best performance in two years.

▲French Fans Celebrate, Transforming the Court

Cochet's victory lay in his unpredictable tactics. Gregory's groundstrokes were very effective, and Cochet was often pressured by them. However, Gregory could not resist the French player's fierce attacks.

The Exuberance of Cochet, World Tennis Champion, After His Victory

After the match concluded, the French were ecstatic. Umbrellas, straw hats, cushions, and newspapers were thrown onto the court, turning it into a pile of garbage, a remarkable sight.

▲Victory or Defeat Depends Entirely on Doubles

After Great Britain won the tournament in 1912, they overcame all opponents this year to once again reach the final week. However, they fell short, losing 3-2. The key to their failure was the lack of a strong doubles team. France had one strong and one weak singles player, while the two British players were evenly matched. Therefore, the singles matches were evenly contested, and the outcome depended on the doubles match. Whoever won the doubles match would win the championship.

▲Cochet, the French Hero

France's continued victory this year is entirely due to Cochet. Borotra completely failed in both of his singles matches. They relied on Cochet's heroic performance, defeating Austin, then Gregory, and pairing with Brugnon to defeat the British Hughes and Kingsley. He fought for three consecutive days, winning all three matches. If France can maintain its victory for another year, it will be solely due to Cochet's efforts.

Special Article

A New Aspect of Chinese Education

—Central Political School (II) by Ye Xing

In addition, there are several affiliated special classes, such as the Xikang Student Special Training Class, with a total of thirty-three students. The four-month training has already been completed and the students have graduated. There is also the Verification Personnel Training Institute, with a total of twenty-eight students. The six-month training has also been completed and the students have graduated. The Mongolian, Tibetan, and Overseas Chinese Student Special Training Class has a total of twenty-four students. The two-and-a-half-year training will be completed this year. Among these three affiliated special classes, the Mongolian, Tibetan, and Overseas Chinese Student Special Training Class has the longest training period and therefore the best results. There is also a Mongolian and Tibetan class, which began training last October, with fifty-four students training for two years. The education in this special class, in addition to focusing on general social sciences, particularly emphasizes issues such as agriculture and animal husbandry, in order to prepare for the reform of the nomadic life and society in Mongolia and Tibet. Another Overseas Chinese class will be established in the second half of the year, recruiting young Overseas Chinese from various regions. However, this class has not yet been formally established. Recently, in order to promote the establishment and reform of national statistics and accounting, and to provide university graduates with specialized knowledge and skills, so as to provide a career path, the National Government has repeatedly discussed the establishment of special statistics and accounting classes by the Central Political School, recruiting university graduates. The training period will be one and a half to two years, with strict training. After graduation, the National Government will dispatch them to work. However, due to insufficient school buildings, it has not yet been opened. It is possible that these two special classes will be opened after a considerable period of time.

Because of the school's strict discipline and good academic atmosphere, everyone wonders how it can be done, but they do not pay attention to its educational policy. The current educational work of the Central Political School is integrated with the academic affairs. There is an educational committee, which is responsible for guiding students' academic studies, cultivation, and extracurricular activities. The school believes that military training is an important part of the entire education. Therefore, the school's military training is not just military drills, but also includes the most important part of military training: military management. The students are organized into a large team, which is further divided into several teams and several squads. People with military knowledge and long-term military training are responsible. It not only pays attention to form, but also to the spirit of the military, cultivating the important virtues of soldiers such as neatness, solemnity, hard work, endurance, agility, and simplicity. The students' lives are very disciplined. For example, every day at 6:00 AM, after the wake-up call is played, everyone must get up, and the squad leader leads the running. After the class bell is played, everyone goes to class, and there is no tardiness or absenteeism. When the meal bell rings, the whole group gathers on the playground, forms a team, and enters the dining hall in an orderly manner. Before hearing the bedtime bell, the dormitory is quiet, with no one to be seen. After the bedtime bell, all the students are in the dormitory, enjoying their sweet dreams. Therefore, the students' actions and habits are very disciplined and orderly. The students' lives in the school, in addition to seeking knowledge, are also a very united military life. The organization of the dormitory and the arrangement of the beds—this is what is called internal affairs in the military—are very regular and must be checked by the squad leader every day. Because neatness and uniformity are required, the uniforms and military blankets are issued by the school. Tuition and accommodation fees are of course not charged, and there is also a monthly food allowance of eight yuan and a subsidy of three yuan.

A Word of Insight

—碧波 (Bi Bo)

▲ The May 3rd Massacre. Occurred within the country. And there is nothing to be done about it. Applying this to the other case, the result of the Korean incident is foreseeable.

▲ "Organized". "No preparation". Although the rhyme is inharmonious, it is an exquisite antithesis.

▲ Natural disasters are incessant. Internal strife is frequent. Although the people do not wish to lie on firewood and taste gall, they are in fact in a position of lying on firewood and tasting gall.

▲ The lives of people in weak countries are cheaper than the livestock of strong countries.

▲ The heavier the pressure, the more violent the reaction. Therefore, those who flaunt their power will eventually be overthrown.

▲ International law is entirely designed for the great powers. What does it have to do with weak nations?

▲ In this world, morality is not to be considered. If there is money to be shared, what is there to worry about selling out the country?

▲ A thing must first rot before insects are born. A man must first insult himself before others insult him. The words of the sages are more profound in this world.

▲ Paying one gold coin to have a prostitute serve wine, she leaves in less than half an hour. For the same price, you can embrace a dancer three times. In the dance hall, even if it is not intended to be prosperous, how can it be avoided?

▲ A person who is stern and stubborn to others on the outside often becomes like a docile cat once inside the boudoir.

▲ Our way of dealing with the world is like throwing something into a pot. If the heat is low, we worry that it will not be cooked; if the heat is high, we fear that it will be scorched. It is difficult to avoid the disease of being overly ambitious or falling short.

▲ The face of the post office, though solemn like an ancient saint, does not refuse even love letters thrown into it.

Recent Situation in Nepal and a Brief History of Its Initial Submission

— Tian Hen

Since the news of Nepal's invasion of Tibet spread last year, the people of the country have begun to pay attention to this small country in East Asia, knowing that although it is small, it is still a completely autonomous country in East Asia. We have often admired Siam for being able to do what we cannot, actually abolishing unequal treaties and regaining consular jurisdiction. Unexpectedly, Nepal, located between India and Tibet, has repeatedly suffered from the aggression of powerful England, but has never yielded, signing an equal treaty of peace. To this day, the British still dare not covet it. Compared with Siam, it is in a different league. And the so-called "upper country" of divine and bright descendants has declined to this point. Is it not shameful? Nepal, also known as Gurkha, is located on the southern foothills of the Himalayas. Its area is more than 50,000 square miles, about the size of our Jiangsu Province. The capital is Kathmandu. The population is about six million, half of whom are Gurkhas who believe in Brahmanism, and half are Nepalis who believe in Tibetan Lamaism. Political power is in the hands of the Gurkhas. Under the king, there are seven chief officials in charge of military, political, financial, legal, agricultural, industrial, and commercial affairs. The standing army is only 80,000 men, stationed in various places. There is also a guard army of 20,000 men, protecting the capital. There is also a bodyguard army of 10,000 men, guarding the palace. There is also an iron cavalry guard of 5,000 men, wearing ancient armor, with a sword on the left side of the waist and a short cannon on the right. There is also a reserve army of 100,000 men. They are not questioned in peacetime as farmers or merchants. However, they must drill three times a year. In case of emergency, they can be called into the army in a moment. The whole country is mountainous, so there are no railways. The capital is also located between two opposing mountains. There are only mountain climbers as a convenient means of transportation. There are a total of eight factories in the country, manufacturing ancient swords and new-style guns. The swords produced are sharp and durable, famous throughout the world. After the British army swallowed Bhutan, they wanted to annex Nepal, thinking it was a small country, a thing in a bag. Unexpectedly, the Nepalese army was brave and good at fighting, and because of the terrain, the Nepalese army climbed mountains and crossed ridges as if walking on flat ground. The British army had never learned this before, and they failed repeatedly. They finally signed an equal treaty, recognizing Nepal as a completely autonomous country in East Asia, to this day. Nepal used to be a vassal state of our country, and still cherishes the Han virtue. Therefore, they treat the Han people very well. They are arrogant to the British, and the British can do nothing about it. Today, we Han people are quite pleased that Nepal is our vassal state. But very few people know the history of its initial submission. Therefore, I have also recorded it. The matter was in the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty. The country was originally inhabited by barbarians. It was divided into the Ye Leng, Bu Yan, and Mu San divisions. Later, the western chieftain Bu La merged them and called it the Gurkha country. At that time, the Panchen Lama was the sixth. Because Emperor Gaozong was celebrating his birthday, he came to Beijing to offer congratulations and received a lot of rewards and donations from princes and ministers. Just as he was about to return to Tibet, he suddenly fell ill with smallpox and died. His followers took his remains back for burial. The assets were swallowed up by the Panchen Lama's brother, Zhongba Hushi Ketu. Not only did he not donate to the temple, but his brother, Marpa, could not share a penny. He was indignant and entered Gurkha, inciting them to invade Tibet. Emperor Gaozong first ordered the bodyguard Bazhong, generals E Hui and Chengde, and others to assist Tibet in suppressing Gurkha. Bazhong and others were afraid of trouble and did not fight. They negotiated with the Gurkha king, inducing him to send envoys to pay tribute, with the condition that Tibet would pay 5,000 taels of gold a year. They also did not clearly inform Tibet. The Gurkha army temporarily withdrew, and Bazhong and others also returned. Later, the Gurkha king asked Tibet for annual tribute. The matter was exposed. Emperor Gaozong was furious and ordered Duke Jiayong, Fukang'an, to be the general and Duke Chaoyong, Hailancha, to be the advisor, and launched a large-scale expedition to Gurkha. Hailancha was a famous general at that time. He won every battle. The Qing army went straight into Gurkha. The Gurkha king was desperate and asked for peace. They did not allow it. The Qing army advanced again, directly approaching the capital. The Gurkha king asked India for help. Although they agreed, the troops did not arrive for a long time (at that time, India was already a British colony). The situation became more and more urgent. He had no choice but to humbly seek peace. Fukang'an agreed. It was then established as a vassal state, receiving official seals. A tribute was made every five years. There were no rebellions throughout the Qing Dynasty. In the early years of Xuantong, they still sent envoys to pay tribute, but they stopped because the revolution was obstructed. During the reign of Emperor Gaozong of the Qing Dynasty, the countries of Annam, Burma, Siam, Ryukyu, and Korea all received official seals and offered tributes. How could they have expected what has happened today? Alas.

Lament for Continuous Rain

— Ming Fei

Nanjing has had more than ten days of heavy rain. The streets and alleys are covered with several feet of water. Du Shaoling's lament for autumn rain cannot compare to this sorrow. I write a lament for continuous rain.

The dark clouds gather, unwilling to open. The heavy rain continues, followed by drizzle. The incessant rain has lasted for ten days. Moss grows on the walls of my tall house. The east window is shaded, and the sun cannot be seen. I knew long ago that the strings would loosen, and the zither would become damp. The moisture reaches my fingertips, and the chess pieces are cold. The ink dissolves with the glue and cannot form a juice. Sitting idly, nothing can be done. I want to go out with an umbrella and clogs, but where can I go? The floodwater on Chang'an Avenue is several feet deep. I watch the children merrily pulling boats into the city. The thoroughfares are like this. How are the lanes? Hunger prevents me from leaving my door. Frogs breed in the submerged stove. The people eat fish. I heard that when the post road was built in those years, millions of gold were spent, but they still hated it being too little. The old canals were all cut off. The new canals are too crudely made. Every year the rain gathers and the water does not flow. The residents stand in the headwaters of the ditch. They use the governance of the people as a pretext for their greed. Sea merchants boast about talking about Yingzhou. Yingzhou is separated by misty waves. They imagine fairy mountains and startle each other. The blind lead the blind, taking each other on. Only the constant rain confirms their madness. It is over. The old man is deaf and dumb. He only teaches his son to speak Xianbei. He sits high on the city walls and scolds the Han people. He likes to boast about his cloth drum in front of the Thunder Gate.

Nine-Sounding Celestial Bird

— Zhe Cun

The Nine-Sounding Celestial Bird. Commonly called the Nine-Headed Bird. Its appearance is indeed nine-headed, hence the name. The Classic of Mountains and Seas says that it is a type of large sea bird. My hometown is on the coast of the East Sea, about two hundred miles away, close to the Doulong and Xinyang ports. The residents use the cry of the Nine-Sounding Celestial Bird to predict wind and rain. I have only heard its cry but never seen its head. I have only heard it at night and never in the daytime. Its cry is melodious and small, like a group of male and female small birds harmonizing their songs. Wind and rain are sure to follow when it cries, or heavy wind and rain. It is always accurate. Hearing it late at night makes one feel sad. When I was a child, I occasionally heard its cry and was quite frightened. I suspected that it was not far away in the sky, so I ran to my late mother, clinging to her lap and not daring to go to another room. In fact, the cry is very loud. When wind and rain are about to come, they feel an unbearable dryness and itching between their feathers, so they must fly high into the sky and soar over the sea to enjoy themselves. Since they fly so high, their cries can naturally reach far. Those hundreds of miles away who hear it seem to think its cry is not loud. Occasionally, seafarers see it at night, and its wings are enough to cover the sky. Qi Jiguang's New Book of Effective Disciplines contains many accounts of using wind and rain to predict weather, including the saying that the Nine-Sounding Celestial Bird appearing means wind and rain, one cry for wind, two cries for rain, three or four cries for wind and rain to cease, etc. However, its nature is such that it does not rise unless there is wind and rain. Once it flies out and cries, it can be determined that there will surely be wind and rain. The records in Qi's book are still based on real experience. This month, the overcast rain has not stopped for ten days. At night, I hear its cries. The bitter wind and rain have turned everything far and wide into a swamp. The water in low-lying areas has become a disaster. Therefore, I especially record this.

Random Talks on the Lives of American Women (II)

— Ji

Hobbies Two or three years ago, mahjong was once popular in the United States. Women regarded it as a noble game, even forgetting to eat and sleep in order to fight on the square city. But now everyone has abandoned it. American women are inherently mobile. They flock to all novel things like ducks. After the craze passes, no one will consult them. This is fundamentally different from the conservative psychology of Eastern nations. Ordinary women mostly like to smoke and drink. Although the American alcohol ban is very strict, ban it if you will, drink it if you will. They still secretly drink at home. The government has no way to investigate and ban it. Except for middle school girls, university students, family ladies, and professional women almost six out of ten like to smoke. In every university student lounge, you can see many girls smoking. However, they watch what place they are in. They never smoke while walking on the street, playing in the park, or at formal banquets. Because they value politeness most, keep order most, and fear being annoying most. Movies, dancing, and horseback riding are still very popular. Everyone in America knows how to dance. This is a noble entertainment for guests at large banquets and social gatherings. It is definitely not like the ones on the sea that are solely for business purposes and leave social people with an excuse to harm social customs. Second, in terms of sports hobbies, such as golf and tennis, they are very popular. Now summer swimming is even more enthusiastic. On the shore of the Chicago Michigan River, the total number of people swimming every day averages more than 30,000. Analyzing it, six or seven out of ten are women. Although men are less free than women due to occupational relationships, it can also be seen that women have a strong interest in swimming.

▲ Socializing Socializing in the open has long been implemented in American society. Ordinary people think that since men and women socialize in the open, wouldn't many jokes come out in society? In fact, it is not the case. Because they or they are all educated, very polite, and have good character. Between each other, they just break down a layer of estrangement and treat each other with courtesy. The so-called "gentleman respects himself" will not have base thoughts and behaviors. Men know many female friends, and women know many male friends, but they are limited to friendship. They will not be involved in love or marriage. It can be seen that the more opportunities men and women have to contact each other in normal times, the more they can avoid many unexpected problems. Otherwise, if both sides cannot understand each other, they will think that everything about the opposite sex is mysterious, and arouse the impulse of curiosity. Therefore, thinking that "socializing in the open" is wrong is a wrong view. Five years ago, the number of female students and male students at Northwestern University in the United States was in a ratio of three to one. The reason is that there are many wealthy families in the nearby villages, and women have the opportunity to receive a university education. At that time, there were naturally more opportunities for male and female students to socialize. According to the speculation of ordinary people's psychology, wouldn't it give the male students the convenience to woo love? However, according to the results of the survey, male and female students have never had a fact that someone fell in love with someone. It is enough to see that socializing is socializing. Love is love. The two cannot be confused into one. Every Saturday, various gatherings are held in any university in the United States to connect the feelings of classmates and relax their exhausted spirits. There are so-called class reunions, fraternities, sororities, etc. There are many interesting entertainments in that kind of meeting, such as tea parties, chats, music, dancing... etc., everything is available. Both men and women go to class reunions. Fraternity members can bring their girlfriends. Sorority members can also bring their boyfriends. The interaction between the sexes is completely free. However, parents still have some restrictions on women under the age of twenty who have not graduated from middle school and who have weak knowledge and abilities.

Rotary Club Storytelling

Woman, Woman (II)

— Yao Sufeng

Miss Ding returned home, feeling a little isolated. Her father had passed away long ago, and only she and her mother were left in the family; in addition, there was a hired maid, Qiu Zi.

Qiu Zi was quite lovable: she seemed like Miss Ding's younger sister, and Mrs. Ding also loved her. Usually, when Miss Ding was at school, Qiu Zi often took care of everything at home alone. Mrs. Ding was forty-five years old, and her daily life was just reciting scriptures and worshiping Buddha. She didn't like to interfere with other things. Miss Ding, on the other hand, was not so much a pampered girl as an innocent child. Her lively personality and beautiful face received the admiration of many people, and she was the target of everyone's attention at school; but she herself didn't take it to heart.

Only she herself knew, and perhaps Qiu Zi knew a little, that she also had some closer friends. Because during the holidays, whenever there was a phone call or a letter, Qiu Zi always received it first. What she often found strange and delighted was that the person who called Miss Ding was often a male voice, saying that his surname was "Li;" and the letters that were sent sometimes came one a day, and sometimes even two a day. The envelope was always written with "Li Jian."

Therefore, Qiu Zi often joked with Miss Ding: sometimes, when she heard the doorbell ring, she would say, "Mr. Li is here:" sometimes, she would even laugh and ask Miss Ding to see Mr. Li's picture. Miss Ding never got angry. In this way, in Qiu Zi's expectation, the facts became even clearer. Therefore, the question of "What kind of person is Mr. Li after all" had powerfully occupied Qiu Zi's expectations.

One evening, Qiu Zi was wandering idly in front of the door. Suddenly, a young man in a suit stood in front of her. She immediately felt that this was a stranger she had never known; but at the same time, in her quick comprehension, she had already affirmed that this unknown guest was Mr. Li she had been expecting.

"Is this Ding Mansion? Is Miss Ding at home?" the young man had already asked.

"Yes! Miss is at home! What is your honorable surname?" Qiu Zi laughed to herself; she later thought that this last sentence was redundant.

However, the visitor's answer finally exceeded Qiu Zi's expectations. When the sound of "My surname is Lu" was softly uttered from the young man's mouth, Qiu Zi was really a little strange.

"Please come inside and sit down!" Qiu Zi suspiciously led Mr. Lu inside.

After going inside to report, Qiu Zi saw Miss Ding change into a newly made long cheongsam, and lightly applied some powder in front of the mirror. Then she hurriedly walked to the reception room.

▲Not Yet Exceeding Sixty Taels: Yesterday, the 27th, the gold price continued its strong upward trend, fluctuating wildly, unable to advance or retreat, hovering around 755 taels. Reports of Silver Supply Showing Signs of Improvement

The tight silver supply in Shanghai has been a long-standing problem, and it has become even more deserted during this summer season. However, there are reports that the supply will improve later. The main reason is that a large quantity of foreign wheat is arriving in Shanghai, and the money for this cargo urgently needs to be cleared, in a very large quantity. Therefore, the silver call loan rate improved slightly yesterday, and the surcharge on checks even exceeded 1 qian, almost reaching 2 qian. According to those in the industry, the silver call loan rate was originally intended to be raised to around 2 qian yesterday. Because there are not many days left in this month, they feared that the total amount of silver call loans for the entire month would exceed 2 taels, so they forcibly suppressed it in recent days. It is expected to rise after the end of this month. Even without a large increase, it will at least be above 1 qian. If the financial sector has other needs, it is beyond our expectations, and the rise of the silver supply is a matter of course.

Grains: Rice Market is Slowly Rising

▲New Pier: Yesterday the weather cleared and the number of incoming vessels from the interior was still low at about 14 or 15. Sales in the area were still good, with 1400 piculs of thick rice bought by the Changshu and Xixiang local merchants. Prices also rose by three jiao compared to the previous session. Kunshan and Liyang white rice prices rose 0.10 or 0.20 yuan due to brisk sales. Sales of Shibu and Chonggu thin rice remained high and prices rose by 0.50 yuan. Glutinous rice distilleries had extremely good demand causing price to rise. Nankang early rice and premium rice types arrived at good prices of slightly over 0.1 yuan. It is estimated that 5000 shih of Heshui foot rice and new rice from Zhoupu would be arriving in Shanghai over the next five or six days.

▲South Market: Sources were limited to types from Qingjiao 2, Nankang 5, Pinghu 4 and Sutong 3 and 4, with scant supplies at Pudong. Sales were slow in both urban and rural shops due to the clear weather, with little interest from the Ningbo area. Thick, hard rice price were up 0.20 to 0.30 yuan. The previous day's rice were a little slower. Thin rice inventories were slightly higher, but prices were unlikely to rise again after days of sharp increases because of the changing weather. A few Luo Yang premium rice arrivals caused prices to increase because of sharp increase in foreign rice prices, resulting in market increases. Yin rice arrived in short supply and saw good sales with prices up 0.20 or 0.30 yuan.

Clear Weather Results in Weaker Flour Prices

Yesterday, the flour market showed signs of flattening and softening, because the sky had cleared up and sentiment inside and outside the industry was very hot. In addition, foreign wheat quotations showed that Canadian wheat had fallen by about one yuan, and Chicago wheat by about 0.30, 0.40, or 0.50 yuan. Although the international market situation is not currently affecting prices, the results will inevitably flow in. Therefore, people's hearts were seeing weakness, and some buyers had returned to the market to sell. Therefore, the opening prices of each price had fallen by 0.01 yuan compared to the previous day. Subsequently, a certain factory maintained the recent price, intending to sell long-term contracts, and Tianjin gangs also made slight purchases, so the sluggish situation turned stable again. In this situation, it is feared that it will circle around again. The total daily transaction volume was extremely brisk, reaching more than 1.5 million. The result was that this month was 0.0025 yuan lower than the previous week, August was 0.0025 yuan higher, September was 0.0075 lower, October was 0.005 lower, and November-December was 0.0075 lower.

Wheat Prices Plunge

Yesterday, the futures wheat market showed a sharp downward trend, because the sky cleared and foreign wheat quotations showed a large drop. Canadian wheat fell by about one yuan, and Chicago wheat fell by 0.30, 0.40, or 0.50 yuan. This kind of drop was completely an oversupply state, so people's hearts were too shaken, and the selling mood was extremely smooth. The generally floating long positions also quickly returned to sell, and the previous days' rise was completely cut down. This month, only January contracts were trading, and the opening price fell by 0.04 or 0.05 yuan. In the afternoon, speculative floating longs raised the price to 3.78 yuan at one point, with the lowest price at only 0.068 yuan, a difference of 0.01 yuan. The distant months went down all the way, and the degree of decline was very large. This month fell by 0.03 yuan, August-September fell by 0.08 yuan, October fell by 0.06 yuan, November fell by 0.07 yuan, and December fell by 0.06 yuan. Spot wheat was lacking in standard and high-quality goods, and the price rose by 0.02 or 0.03 yuan. Kai Zhi Tang, Kunshan Shuangfeng, Taicang Hengjing, Chongming Penglai, and Yangzhou wheat totaled more than 4,000 bales, with 2,500 bales bought by Fu Xin, 700 bales by Hua Feng, and more than 800 bales by Xin Da.

Over a Hundred Items of Wuxi New Silk Arrive

This year's spring and summer cocoons in Wuxi have been poor, but 80-90% of the silk factories have started work. New silk heads have been transported to Shanghai. Yesterday, factories such as Zhen Yi and Yong Tai transported 155 items of new silk, factory leader's spun silk, soup cocoon, cocoon clothing, etc., all transported back to the warehouses by Shen Zhuang, to be arranged in different styles.

European and American Silk Sales Become Even More Lifeless

Yesterday, the Shanghai white factory silk, American sales remained stagnant, and in places such as London and Lyon, the stock market continued to weaken. The factory side observed and waited, and their enthusiasm for imports was also low. The market was calm. Yesterday, only Samsung imported three bales of cotton yellow reeling silk, and Ke Chang, etc., imported sixteen bales of yellow coarse silk, and the price remained stable.

Needle Embroidery European Sales Continue to Be Smooth

Yesterday at the local foreign tea market, needle-eye green tea from Wuyuan and Tunxi, and other places, British firms such as Jardine Matheson, Harmony, Jinlong, and Tongfu all started searching for goods. Transactions were unusually brisk, and sales prices rose by 0.04 or 0.05 yuan compared to last week. The core goods in the Zhenmei category were slightly more popular, and low-grade goods remained brisk. However, for the upper and middle grade goods, foreign firms could not relax their prices because international import prices were very tight, so transactions remained sluggish.

Recent News from the Wutun Tea Market

When the Shanghai market was selling well and prices were high last month, all the tea firms in the Tun region deeply regretted not having procured more tea. Therefore, at that time, tea prices had risen to over 90 yuan. When the new Zi tea came out, everyone hoped that the Shanghai market would recover and prices would return to previous levels, so they enthusiastically purchased it. The highest asking price was also raised to 70 yuan and some change. Recently, seeing that the Shanghai market has been falling for a long time and it's difficult to recover, and that the price of Zhenmei tea has shrunk, enthusiasm has greatly decreased. Currently, the main focus is on finishing the processing of the purchased tea that is in storage. Tea merchants who have stockpiled unsold new tea are now seeing market prices plummet to 40 yuan per dan, only half of the initial opening price. Most tea merchants are suffering huge losses. The price of unrefined tea has remained relatively high due to the prevalence of flower tea production by shops and estates, and the asking price is still around 25 or 26 yuan. Although this is a decrease of three or four yuan compared to before, it is still the highest price compared to previous years.

Because the production of spring tea in Wu County this year was reduced, most tea firms did not purchase their full quota. Therefore, they competed to buy the new Zi tea. The general sentiment was that although the Shanghai market appeared weak, it would eventually recover. Unexpectedly, the Zhenmei market price continued to fall, and the Russian company's assistance was silent and inactive. The item of high-quality Gongxi tea has had its sales channels interrupted because the quality of the goods did not meet the sales needs of other firms. Those who were optimistic before are now lamenting the unpredictability of the tea market. The Zi tea that general tea merchants and firms stockpiled and hoarded in the past, hoping to profit from speculation, is now unwanted. In recent days, tea merchants who have tea on hand are rushing to tea firms to sell it off. Even though the price has dropped by 30 yuan per dan, most are still unwilling to increase their purchases. Fortunately, there is not much tea in storage on the market, so the impact is relatively small. However, traveling merchants are very anxious because they are unable to sell their tea and the market is quickly becoming outdated.

Piece Goods: Eastern Goods After the Boycott

▲Still Operating in Secret...Some are Repackaged as Parcels

▲Cloth from This Factory: Prices Have Been Rising Rapidly Recently, mainly because since the boycott began, fine cloth and fine twill from Japanese factories have been the first to rise in price, and existing stock has been completely bought up. Although guest merchants have been unable to ship goods as of yesterday, there is still a shortage of existing stock. Blue Chicken is selling for 7 taels and 6 mace and a half, Blue Sun for 7 taels and 4 mace and a half, Trumpet Child for 7 taels and 7 mace and a half, and Blue Flying Fish for 8 taels. There seems to be nothing left to buy, mainly because there is an extreme shortage of equivalent products from Chinese factories to replace them. Fine twill from Chinese factories has soared in price yesterday: Jincheng at 8 taels and 1 qian, Butterfly Ball at 7 taels and 6 mace and a half, an increase of about 6 qian compared to before. Coarse cloth has increased by 1 qian. Nine-pound Five Blessing Cat Eagle are all being sold out of customs for 5 taels, and eleven-pound cloth already requires 5 taels and 6 mace and a half.

▲East and West Piece Goods: The previous two days have been consistently dull. Since Eastern goods were largely seized by the anti-Japanese association, local merchants have been cautious and trading has slowed. However, some merchants have been shipping goods through the post office, and there is a trend along the Yangtze River of repackaging goods with Japanese trading companies to declare them, so even if inspections are strict, they are still operating in secret. The price of goods has fallen slightly, but existing stock is quite scarce, mainly because the stock that was previously stored has been completely sold off. Moganshan Zhigong woolen fabric is still being sought after by Hankou merchants, and existing stock is very scarce. Fine Serge is being purchased by both the Shaoxing and Changsha merchants, Sanyou Pattern is 3 qian and 4 fen, and Huxinting is 3 qian and 5 fen. Western goods are no longer comparable to what they used to be, and it is almost impossible to find common, marketable goods. Yesterday, the Shantou merchants traded more than 50 pieces of Striped Baling cloth, with prices averaging 2 qian and 87 fen, while other transactions have been quiet.

North and South Goods: Orchid Bamboo Branches Arrive Sparsely, Prices Expected to Rise

The first batch of Orchid Bamboo Branches that arrived last week were initially priced at around 50 to 48 taels. Considering the cost of land, this would certainly result in losses. However, the cost of land has not eased and has instead increased, so the market trend has become firmer. It has been found that only ten pieces were imported yesterday on the Jinan wheel steamer, a sharp decrease in supply. Therefore, the market is bound to increase in the future. Black Leaf Branches are selling briskly, and there is even greater hope for price increases. It is predicted that there will be an increase of two or three taels.

Sugar Market: Quotations Quiet, Market Firm

▲Taikoo Sugar Hikes Price by 2 Qian

Yesterday, there were still no dispatches from the sugar-producing regions. Outside of the guild's quotations, the foreign exchange rate increased, showing a slight improvement. Dutch sugar #24 coarse granulated white sugar was traded at 11 taels and 4 mace and a half. Both supply and demand were scarce, and the market remained firm. #20 medium granulated white sugar was 11 taels, #8 Dutch red sugar was 9 taels and 2 qian, and finely ground white sugar was 11 taels and 5 mace and a half. Transactions were also sparse. Taikoo Cart Sugar B mark was quoted at 12 taels, and the futures market was at .05 points, DY mark at 10 taels and 8 qian. The market appeared firm. However, the company's existing stock is now quoted at 2 qian higher, with B mark requiring a price of 12 taels and 3 qian, which is still cheaper than the quoted price of 5 yuan and 6 jiao in Japanese currency.

Local News

He Xiong Reports Victory in Telegram to Shanghai

Mayor Zhang yesterday received a telegram from Commander Xiong from Nanchang, stating: "Respected Commander Zhang Yuejun of Shanghai, The central Jiangxi Red Bandits have been cut into two sections by our army's surprise move from Ningdu and Xingguo, and their strength has been disintegrated. The remaining bandits in the area north of Xingguo are currently being encircled and suppressed. The southern Jiangxi area, which has been deeply entrenched as a bandit stronghold for several years, can be fundamentally cleared in the near future. Notified for your information. Respectfully, Xiong Shiyao." Due to lack of space, Mayor Zhang also received a telegram from General Commander He from Nancheng yesterday, stating: "Respected Mayor Zhang of Shanghai, According to an aircraft report, since yesterday afternoon, our army has successively occupied the bandit nests of Longgang and Gulonggang and is pursuing in different directions. Notified for your information. Respectfully, He Yingqin."

Shanghai Intensifies Defense

▲Headquarters Issued a Confidential Order to Comply

Headquarters recently issued a confidential order to the garrison troops of various counties along the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways, roughly stating: "Having received reports, a large number of Red Bandits have been dispatched from other places to Shanghai and various places along the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou railways, intending to secretly plot sabotage and deliberately cause trouble. At this critical time when the front lines are engaged in an emergency campaign to suppress the Red Bandits, the defense of the rear is particularly important. After receiving the order, the garrison troops in each area must properly defend against and prevent any negligence." Therefore, the military police in Shanghai, after receiving instructions from their respective superior authorities, have invisibly intensified their vigilance and defense in key locations.

Shanghai to Hold a Citizens' General Assembly

▲Location... Public Stadium

▲Date... The 30th of This Month

The Executive Committee of the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Headquarters, based on the reports from various associations across the city, including more than 50 groups such as trade associations and citizens' federations, has requested that at this time of domestic and foreign troubles, the national public, regarding the suppression of the Red Bandits, the campaign against Shi Yousan, and the implementation of economic severance against Japan, should urgently convene a general assembly of all citizens to provide a backing for the government, requesting approval for the record. After a meeting, the following resolutions were made: (1) Approval for the record; (2) The name is designated as the Shanghai Citizens' General Assembly for Suppressing Bandits, Punishing Rebels, Opposing Japan, and Aiding Overseas Chinese; (3) The date is set for 3:00 PM on the 30th of this month; (4) Location: Public Stadium in the Southern City; (5) Procedures: The presidium and venue staff shall be elected by the said assembly itself.

The Vanishing of Japanese Goods in This City

▲Customs Brokers Cease Handling

▲Ships Lack Cargo

Following the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association and the severance of economic ties with Japan, merchants from various regions took advantage of the lack of inspection to purchase large quantities of Japanese goods, causing prices to soar. After inspection measures were implemented and various regions responded, prices of Japanese goods fell. Since transportation and customs brokerage firms refused to handle them, Japanese goods have gradually disappeared. Details of the situation are recorded below.

▲Resolutions of Customs Brokers' Association The Customs Brokers Association convened a special meeting on the 26th regarding the anti-Japanese movement to discuss measures. More than two hundred members attended. The details are as follows: 1. Chairman's report: Chairman Shi Zhikun began by saying that since the Wan incident, Japanese imperialists have incited ignorant Korean people to kill our compatriots residing in Korea. The shocking news spread, causing great indignation throughout the country. Anti-Japanese associations have been organized everywhere, and economic ties with Japan have been severed to awaken Japanese imperialists. Shanghai has also formed an Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association to inspect Japanese goods. This association has always participated in anti-Japanese work and has a clear history. Since all sectors are united against Japan, this association will naturally participate. However, considering the poor results of past anti-Japanese associations and the corruption of a few staff members, patriotic people are sighing. He urged those present to maintain their patriotism and conduct a transparent boycott movement. He asked those present to express their opinions fully. 2. Resolutions on important matters: Regarding the Anti-Japanese National Salvation and Boycott of Japanese Goods, the following was decided at yesterday's members' meeting: (1) The association will organize an inspection team of forty members, who will be volunteers from the industry and will register with the association. (2) For Japanese ports (including Dalian), where no other shipping companies are available for transportation, if there are domestic products being shipped there, the Chamber of Commerce has been consulted for solutions. (3) Japanese goods detained by the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association before the Chamber of Commerce meeting have been requested to be returned. (4) Although there are other shipping companies in Shantou and Xiamen, most of them are handling transit goods, making it necessary to load them on Japanese ships. The Chamber of Commerce has been consulted for solutions. (5) Donations to support compatriots should be made at the discretion of the members. (6) Whether to handle customs declarations for Japanese ships importing goods within five days has been referred to the Chamber of Commerce for a response. (7) Xu Youren was publicly recommended to attend the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's Committee for the Study of Boycotting Japanese Goods, and Shi Zhikun was the review committee member. (8) An announcement was made immediately in the newspaper to stop handling customs declarations for Japanese goods and Japanese ships. (9) An announcement was made immediately to the industry to voluntarily stop using Japanese goods. 3. Announcement of boycott: Yesterday, the association issued an announcement stating that the Wan incident has not been resolved, and the disaster for compatriots in Korea has arrived. All Chinese people cannot sit idly by, and this association has no reason to refuse. A general meeting was convened on July 26, and it was unanimously decided to boycott Japan. From this day forward, all staff members of this association will voluntarily refuse to use Japanese goods and will stop handling customs declarations for Japanese goods and Japanese ships. This announcement is for your information.

▲Announcement from the Seafood Industry Association The Trade Union of the Seafood and Sundries Industry issued an announcement to its members regarding the boycott of Japanese goods, stating that it was an emergency notice. Based on the proposal of the association's temporary members' meeting on July 35 and the resolution of the Chamber of Commerce's temporary members' meeting regarding the registration of Japanese goods, it was unanimously passed at the time. All members were required to provide detailed accounts of Japanese goods imported before July 14 and register them with the association before the 28th of this month. This was to be submitted to the Chamber of Commerce and then registered with the Anti-Japanese Association. After that, they could be sold according to the regulations of the Anti-Japanese Association. Accordingly, this case is recorded and announced. It is hoped that you will check and handle it carefully. Furthermore, please do not sell the previously stored Japanese goods privately, lest you incur blame. As for the time and procedures for future sales, further announcements will be made after the regulations of the Anti-Japanese Association are obtained. Please take note.

▲Shortage of Cargo on Yangtze River Steamers Since the 24th, Chinese merchants have unanimously stopped loading Japanese goods. At the same time, it was agreed that Chinese goods would not be loaded on Japanese ships, and Chinese people would not travel on Japanese ships. Since the 25th, the export cargo of the Japanese Qing Company's Yangtze River ships has sharply decreased. The Nanyang Maru, heading upstream, only loaded over four thousand pieces. Yesterday, the Xiangyang Maru, heading downstream, only loaded six tickets of goods, totaling over one thousand seven hundred pieces. On the same day, the ship went to Hankou without a single piece of Chinese cargo. Except for a batch of sugar transported by Japanese people from Zhenjiang, the remaining cement, yarn, and other goods were less than one thousand pieces and were all foreign goods. Business was only 20-30% of what it was before the 23rd. The British Taikoo Yangtze River steamers were overwhelmed with export cargo. For example, the Wuxue and Wenzhou ships each loaded over twenty thousand pieces.

▲Decrease in Imports of Japanese Goods Since the 14th of this month, Japanese merchants have begun to rush their stockpiles to China. Within ten days, 300,000 bags of sugar, over 30,000 pieces of cloth, and 6,000-7,000 tons of sundries were shipped. The goods for August were also pre-shipped. Recently, as the Japanese goods arriving in Shanghai cannot be re-exported, most of them cannot be declared except for a few inferior goods that are used by Japanese merchants themselves. Large quantities of goods are no longer being shipped. Recently, the Mikasa, Maya, and Tsukuba ships have significantly reduced their cargo arriving in Shanghai.

▲Japanese Attempt to Sabotage The Japanese were quite alarmed by the boycott. Yesterday, it was confirmed that the Osaka Japanese Chamber of Commerce had discussed countermeasures against our country's boycott. It was reported that a telegram was sent to Shanghai to send people to investigate the boycott and rescue methods. On the other hand, various industries in Osaka jointly raised five million yuan to sabotage China's boycott movement and ease the intense economic severance. It is said that the Japanese are already taking steps to handle it.

▲Telegram from the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce sent a telegram to the national chambers of commerce yesterday, stating that since the Wanbaoshan incident, the Korean people under Japanese rule have carried out large-scale, organized massacres of overseas Chinese in Seoul, Pyongyang, Incheon, and other places. The Japanese authorities not only failed to stop it but also helped them commit abuse, issuing instructions, and allowing their henchmen to run rampant. The shocking news spread, causing great indignation. In addition to repeatedly telegraphing the central government to request serious negotiations with Japan and to protect and rescue overseas Chinese, the federation held its 32nd Standing Committee meeting to seriously discuss the matter. It was unanimously agreed that our country is facing many difficulties and foreign insults are constantly arriving. For now, the only way is to sever economic ties with Japan to awaken them. The way to save the country is to actively promote domestic goods. It was resolved to send a telegram to all chambers of commerce across the country, advising all sectors to uphold their conscience and implement the following three points: (1) Absolutely refuse to use Japanese goods. (2) Actively promote domestic products. (3) All factories should process and manufacture products, imitating foreign goods for utilization. Accordingly, this case is recorded and a telegram is sent to all chambers of commerce for their information. It is hoped that you will follow the resolution to resist foreign insults and protect our rights. We earnestly pray. Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce; Su Minsheng, Zhang Yuquan, Lu Guangji, Chen Riping, Li Kuian, Peng Chuli, Standing Committee Members.

▲Telegram from Wujin County Chamber of Commerce The Wujin County Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, stating to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce: Recently, the Wuxi County Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram stating that Japanese goods in the interior of Jiangsu Province are all imported through Shanghai. If Shanghai can check, detain, and completely eliminate them, then there will be no problems in the interior. Please lead and actively proceed to prevent the import of Japanese goods, which will greatly help preserve commerce. In the past, merchants have made mistakes. If we promote automatic anti-Japanese actions, we can avoid unexpected pain, and the boycott can achieve complete results. The Wuxi Chamber of Commerce's view is indeed a fundamental solution, and this association strongly agrees. In addition to complying with your chamber's telegram, notifying all trade associations, and each formulating measures to be submitted to the association for collective discussion and action, this special telegram is sent for your information and guidance. We are deeply hopeful, Wujin County Chamber of Commerce respectfully.

Various Parties Pay Attention to Yu Qiaqing's Remarks

▲Those Who Requested Correction National News Agency: Zhou Hanmei and seventy other citizens of this city sent a letter to Yu Qiaqing yesterday, stating: We respectfully write that after the Korean people's anti-Chinese incident occurred, thousands of our compatriots were killed or injured, and property losses amounted to no less than several million. The damage to overseas Chinese merchants in Korea was particularly severe. The news spread, shocking the country and the world. People from all walks of life in this city mourned the tragic killing of our compatriots and were angered by the rampage of Japanese imperialists. Therefore, they rushed about calling for revolution and promoting permanent economic severance with Japan. The business community in this city, seeing that overseas Chinese merchants were the first to bear the brunt, made the greatest effort in this anti-Japanese national salvation movement. We read your initial remarks, which stated, "This Korean people's anti-Chinese incident is, of course, the result of incitement by the Japanese government. The resolution of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Conference in this city to implement economic severance with Japan is a natural action for citizens. (Omission) If the citizens of this country do not have a thorough awakening this time, then national subjugation is imminent." Your calm and painful words were worthy of the attitude of a revolutionary business leader. All our citizens were filled with admiration. After you were elected chairman of the first meeting of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee in this city, we were even more delighted to have the right person, believing that the past anti-Japanese movements in this city often caused ridicule from our own people and pain from foreigners, only adding to the sad pages of our national history. In the future, under your leadership, the economic severance with Japan would be sustained and thorough, and the national consciousness of the people would be awakened. Our Chinese nation would have the opportunity to wash away the many humiliations inflicted by Japanese imperialists. Who knew that upon reading your recent remarks, we would be extremely disappointed and full of errors and contradictions. We love you deeply and are even more eager for the anti-Japanese movement. We use the qualification of compatriots and the legacy of the beloved and sincere Prime Minister Sun Yat-Sen to tell you: (1) Economic severance is the only effective way for a weak country to deal with a strong country. The non-cooperation movement of the Indian revolutionary leader Gandhi is clear evidence. Japanese imperialism is our country's greatest enemy, which everyone in the country can say. The fact that our country's past anti-Japanese movements have rarely been successful is a matter of deep regret for everyone in the country. You have hoped for a thorough awakening of the people and have vehemently stated that without a thorough awakening, national subjugation is imminent. Yet, in your conversation with the Japanese vice-consul, you said, "This is still preliminary work. If the Japanese authorities can awaken and resolve the matter satisfactorily, then we can discuss it. Otherwise, the people will take second and third steps." How fast and wrong is the change in your attitude and the shift in your position? Do you think that economic severance with Japan started with the Korean people's anti-Chinese incident and will end with the resolution of the Korean people's anti-Chinese incident? Can the loss of life and property of overseas Chinese compatriots in Korea be settled with just a letter of apology and a few thousand dollars in compensation? Even if the Korean case is resolved with satisfactory conditions, can the major humiliations that Japanese imperialism has inflicted on our country in the past be forever forgotten? The blood of the May 30th Massacre has not yet reached you. You are at leisure in Shanghai and have not heard the mournful cries of the souls of the May 30th Massacre? The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee in this city has proclaimed to the world that it will permanently sever economic ties with Japan. Revolutionary people all support this proposition and strive to realize it. As the chairman of the committee, your external remarks stated that if there are satisfactory conditions, we can discuss it. Is this so-called discussion just an apology and compensation? At most, your discussion is just to sign an equal commercial treaty (as seen in your remarks). Is this so-called thorough awakening like this? We cannot help but cry. It must be understood that economic severance with Japan should start with the Japanese imperialists' aggression against our country, the awakening of our people, and end with the completion of our national revolution and the defeat of the Japanese imperialists. You should deeply understand this and correct your thinking. One. In your recent remarks to reporters, you said that the committee elected you as chairman, so you did not attend. Second, you said that the scope of economic severance is too broad and cannot be done by merchants. Third, you said that the chairman should be someone from the chairman's office of the Chamber of Commerce, because merchants are the main body of the boycott. Fourth, you said that you are a member of the Chamber of Commerce and should attend. If the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in this city is just a group of merchants, then the chairman does not necessarily have to be someone from the chairman's office of the Chamber of Commerce. If the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association in this city is only attended by merchants, then it is still possible to say that the scope of economic severance is too broad. However, since the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee in this city is organized by people from all walks of life, its task is definitely not just to boycott. The main body of the committee is not any one sector that can claim it for itself. You have avoided attending because you were elected chairman, which is even more ridiculous. The complexity and confusion of your thinking is truly unfathomable. Why do you make such pompous remarks in the newspapers? You should carefully study this and correct your errors. Two. Looking back at your remarks, you said repeatedly that the boycott must be voluntary by merchants and that it should be based on conscience. Alas, it is already pathetic that the boycott requires being passive. It is even more important to encourage people to be voluntary and to regulate their conscience, as the flow of human desires is overwhelming. We do not dare to say that the education of merchants in this city is generally low and that morality is generally degenerate. However, the fact that inferior Japanese goods are selling well as soon as the anti-Japanese call rises can be used to determine that there are indeed many unscrupulous merchants in this city who are mixing and running rampant. You love merchants deeply and encourage them to be voluntary and to regulate their conscience, but what can be done if the speaker is moral but the listener is lawless? Taking Japan as an example, what is the education and morality of Japanese merchants compared to the education and morality of our country's merchants? During the period when the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee is actively inspecting goods, why do you not reflect on this and speak lightly? What will be the impact on the future of the anti-Japanese movement if you advocate voluntary boycott? Because you advocate voluntary boycott, you strongly oppose the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee's detention of goods. One is that those who operate Japanese goods suffer undeserved disasters. The other is that the procedures are too hasty. Before the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee detained the goods, did they issue a notice to those who had purchased them to register with the committee first? If there was such a notice, then it is indeed an undeserved disaster for unscrupulous merchants to secretly transport goods without registering and then have them detained. The work route of the anti-Japanese movement is indeed the correct way. All notices must be transferred through the Chamber of Commerce. Is this the first clause of Mr. Yu Qiaqing's Chamber of Commerce regulations? As the chairman of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee, you are so reckless in your remarks. It is a cause for great sigh. You should pay serious attention to this and seek immediate correction. Three. The other day, the Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special City Party Department published an article entitled "Understanding and Efforts to be Made Regarding the Korean People's Anti-Chinese Incident," which stated, "Unite all oppressed peoples in the world and countries that sympathize with our country to carry out a heroic and death-defying resistance against the barbarous and arrogant Japanese imperialists." We hope that you will take advantage of this great opportunity to go to Japan, unite with the people who have expressed goodwill towards our country, and resist the barbarous and arrogant Japanese government. That would be fortunate. Even if you hire 20,000 to 30,000 people who are friendly to us, the people of our country will surely find great comfort. Alas, the misfortune of the times has already descended. Our country has the rebellion of the Red Bandits and the New Warlords in the south, and the worry of the imperialist Shi Yousan in the north. Major floods are afflicting all parts of the country. The national economy and the people's livelihood are haggard. The rural economy is collapsing. National politics are stagnating. Social order is chaotic. In the midst of encirclement and attack, we actively struggle and swear to resist. The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Committee in this city is entrusted with the position of chairman, such as you. We hope that you will take care of it. How fortunate. We express our views frankly and hope that you will understand. Respectfully addressed to Mr. Yu Qiaqing, Zhou Hanmei, Ren Bin, Yao Yunbo, Zhu Shujian, Cao Huaqiu, Zhang Hanyun, Yuan Qingping, Gu Yufei, Chen Ming, Qian Yongkang, Zhu Chaoran, Zhou Lin, Zhang Hongwei, Li Bingjun, Wu Guangming, Ding Junchuan, Zhou Ziju, Lu Hongru, Tan Si'an, Han Junming, Lu Shujie, Xie Guisheng, Fei Yongzuo, Gu Mingzhai, Lu Qiutian, Lu Heng, Zhang Xiuxiong, Peng Yongjie, Xu Xiyu, Tao Shuyuan, Wei Fei, Yang Baying, Pan Ziyu, Wu Yicheng, Wu Yiheng, Xu Ziling, Kang, Zhang Tingxiang, Shen Zuoren, and seventy other citizens.

▲Those Who Based Their Arguments on Principles National News Agency: The Transportation Industry Association, the Merchant Guild, and the Customs Brokers Association jointly sent a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, stating that the Wan incident has not been resolved, and the disaster for overseas Chinese in Korea has continued. All citizens are deeply indignant, and how can we sit idly by? However, merchant groups are all under the jurisdiction of your association, and we follow your lead in everything. The Entire Beijing-Shanghai Railway is Open

▲Ticket Sales Resumed as Normal This Morning

▲However, Through Tickets for Intermodal Transport are Temporarily Suspended

Regarding the interruption of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway due to rain, after the Railway Bureau's Transportation Department dispatched foreign engineers Li Qiwei and Desifu to work with Chinese engineers Yin Zhilu and others stationed in the Beijing-Zhenjiang section to dredge and repair it, the roadbed between Beijing and Zhenjiang was repaired and reopened the morning before yesterday. The section from Zhenjiang Station to Zhenjiang South Gate Station was also repaired successively by 11 or 12 o'clock the night before last. Therefore, the northbound night express train that departed from Shanghai at 11:45 the night before last could also pass through normally at 5:45 this morning. As a result, the entire railway traffic was completely restored. However, the northbound night express train that departed from the North Station the night before last only sold passenger and freight tickets to Zhenjiang South Gate Station because the Transportation Department was not sure whether the tracks in the Zhenjiang area could be repaired on time. Ticket sales resumed as normal at 5:15 this morning. However, through tickets for Shanghai-Suzhou intermodal transport and Beijing-Shanghai-Tianjin-Pukou through tickets are still temporarily suspended and will be restored after receiving notices from the Tianjin-Pukou Railway and Suzhou Kunshan and other places.

Guangdong Authorities Underpay Customs Revenue

▲Inspector General of Customs Orders Guangdong Customs to Pay

National News Agency: The Inspector General of Customs stated that the customs revenue remitted to Shanghai by the Guangdong Customs has recently been only a portion of the old customs duties and is not sufficient to cover the principal and interest of various domestic and foreign debt indemnities that should be apportioned. Recently, the Customs Commissioner of Guangdong Customs was instructed to contact the Guangdong authorities and pay the amount that should be paid as scheduled. The original order is as follows: "For compliance, it is found that when the Guangdong government intercepted the customs duties of Guangdong and Guangxi, it declared that the expenses of customs collection within the territory of the two provinces of Guangdong and Guangxi and the foreign debts secured by customs duties, as well as the indemnities of various countries, would still be allocated as before. Although on May 30 of this year, the Guangdong government telegraphed the whole country, stating that it did not recognize the laws and regulations promulgated by the National Government after May 28. On June 15, the Guangdong Provincial Standing Committee members Tang Jun Shaoyi, Wang Jun Jingwei, Sun Jun Ke, Gu Jun Yingfen, and Xu Jun Chongzhi jointly sent a letter to various banks and the custodians of public debt funds across the country, stating that although the government did not recognize the laws and regulations issued by the National Government after May 29, the various domestic bonds issued before May 28 should still be considered valid, and all procedures should still be handled according to the usual method. According to this, the Guangdong government has already recognized that the customs duties of the Guangdong and Guangxi provinces are liable for debts incurred before May 28 and should continue to be fulfilled as before. There is no doubt about this. The number of customs revenues from the Guangdong and Guangxi provinces is calculated according to the total revenue for the entire year of 19 and from January to April of this year, accounting for approximately 11.5% of the national customs revenue. The indemnities, domestic and foreign debts, and the principal and interest payable on various treasury bills issued before May 28 that should be allocated by this Inspectorate General of Customs this year, which are secured by customs duties, total approximately US$38,204,000, which is equivalent to 95,510,000 Customs Gold Units, and domestic debt is approximately 114,677,700 silver dollars. Therefore, the 11.5% of the amount that should be borne by the Guangdong and Guangxi provinces each month is approximately 915,000 Customs Gold Units and 1,100,000 silver dollars. Currently, it is found that since June 11 of this year, after the Guangdong authorities intercepted the customs duties, the customs revenue remitted to Shanghai by the Guangdong Customs has only been a portion of the old customs duties. The newly added and additional tax portions have all been intercepted. Therefore, for the month of June, the customs duties remitted by the various customs offices in the Guangdong and Guangxi provinces for various debt indemnities only amounted to 1,103,846 yuan. Furthermore, for the month of July, as of July 15, only 196,123 yuan of customs revenue has been remitted. The customs revenues remitted by the various customs offices in the Guangdong and Guangxi provinces are not sufficient to cover the principal and interest of various debt indemnities that should be paid. Therefore, you, the Customs Commissioner, are ordered to immediately contact the Guangdong authorities in writing in accordance with the above-mentioned intention and urge them to immediately make up for the previously underpaid customs revenues and to ensure that the amount that should be paid is paid in full in the future without delay. You are still ordered to report the reasons for the previously short-paid customs revenues and the results of the contact in detail by telegram. This order," etc.

Graduation Ceremony Held at the Local Self-Government Training Institute Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Local Self-Government Training Institute, attached to the Shanghai Municipal Government, which was established in December of last year, its first class of students has completed its three-month training and three-month internship. Yesterday morning at 10:00, the Municipal Government held a graduation ceremony at the Diplomatic Ministry's Shanghai Office Building. Mayor Zhang, Director Yu (Secretary-General Yu), Deputy Director Ji Zongxing, Municipal Government Counselor Sun Baorong, Secretaries Guo, Geng Jiaji, Tang Tuxuan, etc., all teaching staff of the training institute, special class students, ordinary class students, about 200 people, attended. After that, Mayor Zhang personally presented graduation certificates. A total of seventy-six ordinary class graduates and one hundred and five special class graduates received certificates.
