Social News

After Watching the Joint Photography Exhibition

— Guangmei

Although it cannot be said to be an unprecedented initiative, it is a very rare opportunity. Shanghai, which ranks first in civilization in the country, can often see exhibitions of Chinese and Western paintings, but photography exhibitions are not common. A long time ago, the Times Museum held a photography exhibition, and I was also one of the visitors. Unfortunately, the only impression it gave me was admiration for the author's superb skills, and nothing else special. In fact, even such an ordinary exhibition cannot be seen often.

Suddenly giving us a long-desired request, the Joint Photography Exhibition is open for two weeks at the Jiande Apartment on North Sichuan Road. The main authors are Mr. Lu Shifu and Mr. Lang Jingshan. The research and artistic excellence of these two gentlemen in photography have long been admired by the general public. However, I have to be surprised and amazed at Mr. Lu's achievements. It turns out that Mr. Lu Shifu is a well-known German doctor, but I never thought that he would be so accomplished in photographic art.

In previous photography exhibitions, we only saw landscapes, still lifes, and jade shadows of beautiful modern girls, but rarely saw attention to the human body. Human body photography can be said to be difficult to find. In the works of Mr. Lu and Mr. Lang, they paid a lot of attention to this aspect. In Mr. Lu's works, nudes and beauties are especially numerous. For example, "Shame" is an extremely beautiful painting. From this exhibition, I resolutely eliminated my long-held dogmatic prejudice that photography is not as easy to express as painting. I am now saying this: photography and painting are not inferior to each other. As long as you get the right method, they are equally vivid. This correction was given to me by Mr. Lu and Mr. Lang. I should be grateful.

Mr. Lu and Mr. Lang are able to pay attention to the human body, which is of course worthy of admiration. However, there is one thing, the human body works on display are all female, which is a small issue worth discussing. I hope that Mr. Lu and Mr. Lang can pay attention to the male aspect in the future, and express the strong and brave male beauty. At the same time, I hope that in the next exhibition, there will be more dazzling works on display in front of our eyes.

Soviet Russia Dumps Kerosene in Dong Province

Also plans to dump matches, timber, and flour

Shenyang News: The Russian Trade Branch stationed in Shenyang, under the instructions of the government, is dumping kerosene in Dong Province, and has entrusted the Chinese merchant Hong Shun Sheng Company in the city as the general agent. It is reported that the Russian side will then dump matches, timber, flour, and other items, depending on the performance of Hong Shun Sheng Company.

Global Military Spending Increases by 100 Million US Dollars

China 94 Million US Dollars

New York News: According to the Boston World Peace Association, global military spending in the past fiscal year amounted to 4.158 billion US dollars, an increase of approximately 100 million US dollars over the previous year. The country with the highest military spending in the past fiscal year was the United States, with 773.2 million US dollars, followed by Russia with 579 million US dollars, third was France with 466.98 million US dollars, fourth was Britain with 466.525 million US dollars, fifth was Italy with 248.94 million US dollars, sixth was Japan with 236.86 million US dollars, seventh was Germany with 171.92 million US dollars, and eighth was China with 94.29 million US dollars. Also, on the mainland, Europe, with 28 countries spending 2.56311 billion US dollars, was the highest, followed by North and Central America with 12 countries spending 795.91 million US dollars, South America with 10 countries spending 171.94 million US dollars, Africa with 3 countries spending 15.9 million US dollars, and Asia and Australia with 8 countries spending 61.45 million US dollars.

New Survey of American Movies

Investment of 500 Million US Dollars, Exports of Over 200 Million Feet

According to American newspapers, the average daily transaction of films in the American film industry reaches 2,500 miles, which, when extended, is enough to circle the earth. Also, 18 million people enter the cinema every week. Due to the transformation from silent films to sound films, the amount invested in the film industry in the past year for equipment and other expenses totaled 500 million US dollars. On the one hand, the year 1930 indicated that sound films conquered silent films. From January to September, the United States exported 210 million feet of film, of which about 118 million feet were sound films, accounting for about 67 percent, and silent films accounted for about 33 percent.

US Beet Harvest Reduced by More Than 10%

Due to Production Restrictions

According to the US Department of Agriculture, the cultivation of US beets in 1931, surveyed on July 1, was 84.7%, and the harvest was forecast to be 7.57 million tons, a decrease of 1.8% in cultivation and a decrease of 1.605 million tons (18%) in harvest compared to the previous year, due to production restrictions.

The Life of Working Women in New York

— Lin

(Continued from yesterday)

Clara arrived at the hotel five minutes late. She found this to be a very enjoyable act, because it could show the spirit of independence. She didn't have to swipe the time clock. She locked her coat and hat together and then strolled naturally through the hall. Many people watched her. From her expression, it seemed that she was indifferent to all the attention. In fact, she was not. The girl she was replacing was eager to leave. She had started work at six in the morning and was now very hungry. She greeted Clara very warmly. They didn't have much friendship, but they were very trustworthy. They worked together for several hours every day, so naturally everyone had some secrets to tell. Secretly, everyone was jealous. If someone wore a new dress, the other would eagerly admire it, but secretly she was very jealous and wanted to outdo her. Clara's colleague was named Luo Xuetuo. She was very proud of her name.

Clara stood behind the counter to take over her duties and automatically began to tidy up the display windows.

"Busy?" she asked Luo Xuetuo.

"Ah, yes, no. The manager told me that there will be a big gathering next week. Anyway, we can always find a meal there." These women have learned a special skill to dig for gold. They have ways to ask men to take them to dinner and to the theater. The lobby of the hotel is indeed a wonderful place. They can quickly and accurately judge a person. They are unwilling to go out with stingy people. They don't mind being patted on the cheek or secretly kissed. These women know how to take care of themselves. Their appearance is very stubborn, and their hearts are as hard as their appearance. Every day, hundreds of young people with confused ideals pass through the lobby of a big city hotel, seeking to live without any blows or traumas. Therefore, the only way to treat people is with a cynical attitude. Clara also does this, but there is still some reservation. The background of her soul is a beautiful and romantic picture, but there are still reservations. Clara knows that love alone is not enough for her. Love must be combined with money.

Men stand outside the cigarette counter and talk every day. Most of them are just deceiving the girls, or teasing them a little. The initial expression of radical men cannot be separated from the sentence "Where have you been all my life?" The answers to this sentence are different, depending on how the girls know them. Clara might say, "I've been waiting for you here until that lucky day comes," or "I won't go anywhere else in my life."

Some men tell the girls many secrets, business difficulties, and past experiences. The girls are very sensible. There are very few people who live in the hotel permanently. Most of them are temporary travelers and returning guests. The girls recognize the guests who leave and come back often.

The time Clara spends standing at the counter passes very quickly. She often feels like she is on the stage, playing a role. She studies every move she makes. When she changes shifts to eat, at three o'clock in the afternoon, she has bad luck, because she must take out her own money to buy food. How happy she would be to run to the hotel's tea room, order a salad, some meat, ice, and coffee, and not have to pay for it herself. There is a Chinese chop suey restaurant across the street. For fifty cents, you can get a full meal, plus a dime for the tip. Clara runs to this restaurant. She doesn't want to pay so much money for a meal. However, she speculates that she often spends a lot of money on food. If she often eats by herself, she doesn't know how she will live. A bedroom costs fifteen yuan per week, and each person has to pay seven yuan and five cents. There is also the cost of the public bus, and the most is clothing. Broadway is not like Fifth Avenue, which is the center of clothing styles. They know the effect of clothes and use clothes to please others. In the hotel, they have to wear dark clothes. Clara often uses satin to make clothes. She likes cute socks and boots, especially patterned boots and shoes. Somehow, she breaks boots and shoes more easily than other girls. This expense is not small. (To be continued)
